An Analysis of China's Recent Finances (Continued) 45

— Sun Huairen

From the perspective of China's revenue, the imbalance of finances seems to have become an incurable cancer. To remove this cancer, there are only two means: one is to find a way to increase the gradually decreasing tax revenue; the other is to see if there is a way to cut expenditures. If both of these means fail, then the future of China's financial economy will be very pessimistic.

Here, we will first discuss the possibility of improving revenue.

In our previous narratives, which discussed finance in terms of finance, the situation of tax revenue is indeed getting worse. To change this situation in the future, we should naturally start by improving the root of taxation – the national economy. Generally, people who are optimistic about the legal tender policy believe that the legal tender policy can take on the responsibility of improving the root of taxation. They believe that after the implementation of the legal tender policy, the value of China's currency has decreased by about 25%. As a result of this currency depreciation, prices can be raised. As a result, most of China's farmers can sell their agricultural products for money, thereby increasing their purchasing power. On the other hand, as a result of the decrease in the value of China's currency, the import of foreign goods can be reduced, and national industries can take the opportunity to prosper, and the prosperity of the industrial and commercial classes is just around the corner. Also, China's export goods can also become prosperous due to the decrease in currency value. These various effects after the decrease in currency value can make the entire Chinese national economy prosperous, thereby making tax revenue gradually increase, and the imbalance in financial revenue and expenditure can be easily solved.

Whether these theories are all true, we will leave aside for the moment, but here a contradiction clearly arises, that is, even if the import of foreign goods can be reduced due to currency depreciation, the revenue from customs duties will naturally decrease as a result. May I ask if there is still a way for Chinese finance, which is built on the foundation of customs duties? Many national debts will not be able to be repaid, and how will revenue and expenditure be balanced? As for saying that the import of foreign goods will decrease and national industries can prosper, this is also impossible in reality, because the flow of international funds is running towards countries with falling currency values. Even if the import of goods from various countries decreases, the inflow of foreign capital will probably increase. Then, using their right to set up factories locally in China, they will launch fierce attacks. At that time, national industries will not only not prosper, but may even have no peers. Recently, many people have been using the upward trend of the production index compiled by the Central Bank (the average in 1935 was 102.1, and in June of this year it was 105.7) to prove the prosperity of industry. This argument is absolutely wrong. It should be known that the Central Bank's production index is compiled based on the materials from the Consolidated Tax Administration. Therefore, most of it is the production of foreign-owned factories, not the so-called national industries. Specifically analyzing various production indexes, we can even know that the product whose index has risen the most is beer (the average in 1935 was 101.1, and in June of this year it was 213.9), which has risen by 112.8%. The index that has not only not risen but has instead fallen is flour (the average in 1935 was 113.5, and in June of this year it was 82.4), which has fallen by 31.1%. This is because most of the beer is foreign-owned, while almost all of the flour is Chinese-owned. So how can this production index tell us that national industries are prosperous?

Moreover, in fact, most of China's imported goods are necessities, and currency depreciation may not necessarily be able to prevent their import. Regarding this point, some people have also pointed out recently that imports in the past six months of this year were only 460 million yuan, a decrease of 15.9% compared with the same period last year, and exports were 330 million yuan, an increase of 28.3% compared with the same period last year. Therefore, it is said that the legal tender policy has been effective. However, it is very dangerous to mechanically apply statistical figures in this way. How can we not consider the tens of millions of yuan of smuggling in North China in recent years as China's imports just because it is not included in the statistics? As for the increase in export goods, we should also analyze its contents. It is probably some military raw materials that are unique to China, or some commodities for which there has been a sudden increase in demand in overseas markets, and it has little to do with the depreciation of currency value.

Finally, we want to examine the extent to which the legal tender policy is beneficial to rural areas. Optimists of the legal tender policy believe that the first good result for rural areas is that it can raise agricultural product prices. This point cannot be denied. The following is a comparison of several agricultural product indexes before and after the currency reform:

September 1935 September 1936

Shanghai Agricultural Product Wholesale Price Index 72.27 88.57 (July)

Shanghai Exported Agricultural Product Price Index 74.50 112.20

Shanghai Imported Agricultural Product Price Index 121.10 137.20

From this index, it can be seen that agricultural product prices have indeed risen, but these are, after all, just prices in the city, which are much higher than the selling prices in rural areas. According to a survey by the Central Agricultural Experimental Institute, for example, the difference between the rice price in the producing areas and the consuming areas in various counties in Zhejiang is often in the range of two yuan. The difference will of course be even greater in other inland areas where transportation is more inconvenient. Therefore, the 20% or more increase in agricultural product prices in cities probably has a negligible impact on agricultural product prices in rural areas. Moreover, what we should pay even more attention to is that the agricultural product price import index is still far above the export price index. In addition, the indexes of production goods and consumer goods in the import price index also generally tend to be the same as agricultural products. Therefore, the benefits that farmers get from the rise in agricultural product prices are mostly offset by the losses suffered from the rise in the prices of their consumer goods, and it is difficult to say how much improvement there has been.

From the results of these analyses, it can be seen that the legal tender policy's power to improve the national economy should definitely not be overestimated. Since it is difficult to have significant hope for a significant improvement in the national economy recently, then not only can there be no hope for an increase in tax revenue in finance, but also the tendency for tax revenue to gradually decrease is probably very difficult to prevent. (To be continued)

Spring Planting Season: Gansu Province Strictly Orders Prohibition of Planting Poisonous Plants, County Magistrates Must Personally Enter Rural Areas to Investigate and Prohibit, No Opium Seedlings Allowed to Appear Next Year 46

Lanzhou Correspondence: Yu Xuezhong, Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government, has separately telegraphed orders to the counties of the first, second, and third phases to comply with the prohibition of opium. Now that the autumn harvest has ended and spring plowing is approaching, in order to promote the matter early, a proclamation has been printed and distributed to prevent the people of the entire county from planting opium again. At the same time, orders have been issued to the county magistrates to widely post the proclamation and personally enter rural areas to investigate and eliminate poisonous plants. Instructions on matters that require attention have been provided for effective implementation, so that no opium seeds will enter the soil this year, and no opium seedlings will appear next year, in order to maintain the prohibition policy. The original text of the instruction and proclamation is recorded below: "Regarding the prohibition of opium in this province, it is handled in five phases. The counties in the first and second phases that prohibit the planting of opium seedlings must be completely prohibited in the past two years. The counties in the third phase should implement the prohibition starting from January 1937. Orders have already been telegraphed for compliance. Now that the autumn harvest has ended and spring plowing is approaching, it is urgent to promote the matter early and personally enter rural areas to investigate and eliminate poisonous plants. It is appropriate to print and distribute a proclamation, ordering the county magistrate to widely post it and make it known to all, and to list the matters that require attention for implementation as follows: (1) Widely inform the district and township chiefs to order all households within their jurisdiction who have opium seeds in storage to hand them over within three days, or destroy them themselves, and submit a written guarantee to the county through the layers, and the county will supervise the burning of the handed-over opium seeds and report to the government for record, and send personnel to investigate, and if found again, in addition to confiscating the opium seeds, the holder will be sent to the court for handling. (2) Order the district and township chiefs to warn each household not to plant opium, and supervise to ensure that no seeds enter the soil, and issue a guarantee that no opium seedlings will be found in the future, and submit it to the county for record, and report it to this government for record. (3) Prepare and issue a "Those who plant opium will be severely punished according to military law" simple notice and post it in rural areas, and hold meetings with all sectors of society to expand publicity. (4) If the county territory borders counties that have been slow to prohibit opium, and there are enclaves interspersed in various places, the related counties should be consulted immediately to reorganize according to the province's measures for handling enclaves and exclaves, clarify county boundaries, and report the special case. Exclaves should be completely prohibited regardless of territory, and in enclaves, neighboring counties should be consulted to ensure that no opium is planted within one zhang of the connecting lines with the opium-prohibiting counties, and markers should be set up to avoid mixing. Now that the communists are fleeing west and large armies are gathering, if strict implementation is not carried out and jiahe is planted instead, not only will the poisonous atmosphere be difficult to clear, but also food supplies will inevitably be exhausted. The opium should be complied with and strictly implemented, so that no opium seeds will enter the soil this year, and not a single opium seedling will be found next year, which is of utmost importance. This order,

Precious Items at the Jiang-Zhe Literary Exhibition, totaling over 6,000 varieties and 20,000 items. 47

Hangzhou Correspondence: The Education Department of Zhejiang Province, in order to commend Zhejiang literature, promote academics, and achieve the effect of learning from the past to plan for the future, decided to hold the Zhejiang Literature Exhibition this year. The Provincial Library, which has been focusing on collecting books and documents from the province, was specifically assigned to organize the event. After several months of preparation, it has been completed and officially opened on the 1st of this month. Detailed methods were established for collecting items for the exhibition, and collection branches were set up in the nine administrative regions of Zhejiang Province, as well as in Shanghai, Nanjing, Beijing, and other places. With the support of various public institutions and esteemed scholars from various regions, many types of items were collected. According to the library's announcement, the content includes books, calligraphy, portraits, antiques, rubbings of inscriptions, and revolutionary literature. From the beginning of the collection to the present, over 6,000 varieties and 20,000 items of various cultural relics have been obtained. The most valuable and rare items are categorized and recorded as follows: (1) Manuscripts of Local Worthies, such as Zhang Dai of Shanyin's handwritten "Shi Kui Shu" (said to be plagiarized by Gu Yingtai) and "Tao An Miscellaneous Manuscripts," Chen Hongshou of Zhuji's handwritten first draft of "Bao Lun Tang Collection," Wu Yankuang of Yongjia's "Flower History," Wang Yizhong of Qingtian's "Jing Fei Lu," Zhu Yizun of Xiushui's first draft of "Jing Yi," Qi Zhaonan of Tiantai's handwritten "Yu Zhi Tang Wen Ji," Sun Yirang of Ruian's various original manuscripts, Huang Yizhou of Dinghai's "Jing Li Miscellaneous Works," and Zhang Binglin of Yuhang's handwritten books, etc. (2) Collated Editions, such as Qian Taiji of Jiaxing's hand-copied and collated "Laozi Daodejing," and Sun Yirang of Ruian's collated "Li Qi Tong Gu." (3) Manuscripts, such as Feng Dao Wang's handwritten "Lu Shi Shi Xue" from the Ming Dynasty, Xu Wei's handwritten "Wen Ji Shu Zhuan," handwritten poem drafts by Zhong Huang, Lu Wudang's handwritten drafts of his father's "Wancun Poems" from the Qing Dynasty, and Cha Chuba and Lu Baojing's handwritten poems, which are treasures of the book world. (4) Portraits of Local Worthies are particularly rare, including the portrait of Qian Wusu Wang of Wuyue, as well as the portrait of Yang Cihu of the Song Dynasty (painted in the late Ming Dynasty), Liu Wencheng's "Shi Shou Jing Tu" (painted by Chen Laolian), a combined portrait of seven generations of Wang Wencheng Gong, portraits of Fan Dongming (Qin), Mao Xihe, Jiang Ximing, and Zheng Hancun of the Qing Dynasty, a combined portrait of Xihu and Zhu Zhutuo (painted by Ding Xiaozhi with inscriptions), portraits of Quan Xieshan, and combined portraits of Xieshan and Xinghang Dazong, and portraits of martyrs such as Zhang Cangshui and Qian Zhongjie. There are also countless large photographs taken of other portraits. (5) Relics of Local Worthies, such as Qian Wusu Wang's iron certificate, which could not be obtained despite negotiations, but the Tian Ce Tang jade seal of Wusu is also very valuable. Other items include the painting inkstone of Meihua Daoren of the Yuan Dynasty, Wu Zhonggui of Jiaxing, the court tablet of Wang Huaibin of Yunhe in the Ming Dynasty, the iron helmet used by Zheng Xiao of Haiyan during the defense against Japanese pirates, Zhang Cangshui's inkstone (collected by the Yang family of Cixi and never shown), Leqing Heshanren Baiyi's inkstone, Chen Guifen, the martial arts champion of Tiantai in the Qing Dynasty's Yulin armor, Zhang Shuwei's postscript on the Qin measuring instrument of Jiaxing, and Tao Qibiao's Tao Gong bed and Tao Gong cabinet of Kuaiji, all of which are worthy of cherishing. The relics of revolutionary martyrs are displayed separately from Baiyi's inkstone, etc. (6) A section on National Revolutionary Documents (limited to Zhejiang natives), due to the difficulty of solicitation, the collection is limited. However, items such as the Guangfuhui history written in pencil by Tao Huanqing, the leader of the Guangfuhui, two days before his martyrdom, the secret propaganda materials of Ao Mengjiang of Jiaxing, ancestral teachings, and prayers, and Xu Bosun's early-year map of the Chinese coast are also rarely seen by the Chinese people. The exhibition also includes relics of Qiu Nüxia and portraits of martyrs from Shanyin. Chen Yingshi's blood-stained clothing, treasured by the Lake Society and not easily shown to the public, is also brought here for public viewing through the efforts of the organizers, echoing the bronze statue on the lake. (7) Calligraphy and paintings of local worthies, selected from more than 500 scrolls, are overwhelming in their beauty, whether in the form of scrolls, hand scrolls, or album pages. Notable examples include Wang Wencheng Gong's family letters from the Ming Dynasty, Liu Ji's hand-written notes, Zhen Hezhi's imitation of Mi Zhishui, Ren Dao of Ruian's landscape painting, Wu Cheng's Wusi Xiamu Chuiyin map, Chen Laolian's Xishan Dushu map of Zhuji, Mao Xihe's painting of Yulinglong Stone, Dai Wengong's bamboo painting of Qiantang, and other masterpieces too numerous to mention. Xia Gui and Xia Ze of Qiantang in the Song Dynasty are suspected of being forgeries, and the authentic works of Yue Zhongwu and the correspondence of Ge Xiaoxian of Linhai are not included in the count of the works of local worthies. (8) Printed Books and Documents include the "Bao Qie Tuo Luoni Jing," printed during the Xian De period of the Later Zhou Dynasty, discovered at Tianning Temple in Huzhou (20 years earlier than the Leifeng Pagoda scroll), Song Dynasty Jianben, Chen Jieyuan's bookstore edition, Yuan Dynasty West Lake Academy edition, and fine prints from Zhejiang Province in the Ming and Qing Dynasties, which can be used to view the history of printing in Zhejiang. (9) Collections of Books and Documents, including the collections of Fan's Tianyi Pavilion, Qi's Danshengtang in the Ming Dynasty, Zhu's Shancaitang, and Bao's Zhibuzu Zhai in the Qing Dynasty, as well as Ding's Bachuanjuanlou and Sun's Yumeilou, are all displayed. Rare items include Yan Jiuneng's postscript on Zhou Yigong's manuscript from the Song Dynasty and Wu Meicun's hand-copied "Linpu Zhou Xiansheng Ji" from Shancaitang, which are treasures of the book world. (10) Scientific Documents include a large collection of Ming and Qing Dynasty provincial examination records, and the Ming Dynasty Dengke records from Tianyi Pavilion in Ningbo are also selected and exhibited. The most eye-catching are the original Zhu Juan of Qi Chengrang and Qi Biaojia of Shanyin in the Ming Dynasty, and the silver cup used by Zhang Weichi of Haiyan in the early Qing Dynasty at the Yan Lu Ming banquet in Zhang's Sheyuan, as well as the Jinshi clothing and palace examination papers of Chen Shengqin of Tiantai in the Qing Dynasty collected from Taizhou. (11) There is a large collection of archives, such as the private accusation of Zhang Dajie by the Grand Scholar Hu Zhaolong during the Shunzhi period of the Qing Dynasty, the memorial of the bribery case of Shen Jinshi of Huzhou, the memorial of Ruan Yuan, the governor of Zhejiang in the 14th year of Jiaqing, and the copied drafts of the Yang Naiwu case preserved by Yuhang County, which are also of great value. (12) The collection of Zhejiang local chronicles is extremely rich, including the Song Dynasty editions of "Siming Zhi" and "Chicheng Zhi," as well as the Ming and Qing Dynasty chronicles. In addition to those collected by the Zhejiang Library over the past 30 years, the treasures of Tianyi Pavilion, Jiaye Building, Wufeng Old Hut, the National Library of Peiping, Jinling University, and other private collections are also combined to form a grand spectacle. (13) The charts include 40 newly drawn maps of Zhejiang's historical geography, as well as old maps of Zhejiang Province from the Ming and Qing Dynasties borrowed from the National Library of Peiping. The various economic and transportation maps sent by the construction agencies are not included. (14) The genealogy section includes the family histories of large surnames from various parts of the province in the Ming and Qing Dynasties, which the Zhejiang Library originally collected, supplemented by local borrowings. Among them, the Song Dynasty genealogy treasured by the Chen family of Fengqiao, Zhuji, is the most famous. The first page of the genealogy has the inscription of Emperor Gaozong in the 15th year of Shaoxing, four portraits of Chen Sheng, Chen Zizuo, etc., and the national seal of "Zhang of the Great Song." It is said that Song and Yuan Dynasty genealogy books are quite common, but this is the only one that is generously displayed at this exhibition, making it the most valuable genealogy and a rare sight in the world. (15) There are very few original bronzes and stone inscriptions on display this time. The gilded pagoda of Wuyue and the Tang Dynasty stone scripture pillar are quite precious. The rubbings are collected by the Zhejiang Library over the years and contributed by various parties, and they are very numerous. In addition to the recent rubbings, there are also old objects from the Tang and Song Dynasties. (16) The calligraphy and paintings are not numerous, but there is the Dongyang version of the Lanting Collection, and Wang Shijun's "Luoshen Fu" rubbed from the Chengxintang paper of the Southern Tang Dynasty, borrowed by Mr. Sun Zhifu, is a treasure of the inner court with obvious Zhu Zhang marks. Although it is not specifically related to Zhejiang literature, it is a treasure of this art. The collection of cultural relics is so large that the display was not completed at the time of writing, and the compilation and recording were hasty and flawed. I hope to describe it in detail another day. (Editor's note: The list of exhibits and inscriptions will be published in the special issue of the Zhejiang Library's "Literary Journal," Volumes 3 and 4.)

Current Affairs Commentary

The Black Shirt Premier's Roar 48

— Lang

The roar of the Italian Black Shirt Premier in Milan on the 1st of this month simply shook the hearts of every European. The importance of this speech to the European political situation is not only because it contains many important points, but also because it indicates a new trend in the foreign policy of the Fascist group. The Black Shirt Premier's speech was delivered after the Italo-German talks, so the attitude of Germany can also be seen from Italy's attitude. In other words, Mussolini's speech was actually a revelation of the results of the German-Italian talks. Such a declaration with great significance will undoubtedly have a great impact on the future development of the European political situation.

The Black Shirt Premier's speech, in addition to a part on domestic affairs, covered a wide range of foreign affairs and was very important. Mussolini first attacked the illusions of pacifists, such as the Disarmament Conference, the League of Nations, and the collective peace system. He then explained Italy's attitude towards the Danube River basin countries of Britain and France, as well as communism. Regarding the results of the Italo-German talks, he believes that they are the basis for cooperation between European countries. Let us now analyze some of the key points to speculate on the diplomatic trends of the Fascist group and its relationship with the international political situation.

First, let's talk about Mussolini's attack on the pacifist "illusion." In the world of imperialism, seeking the success of disarmament and forming a truly peaceful League of Nations is an illusion that is not easy to achieve great success. However, we know that in the world of thick gunpowder, the collective security system is still a relatively practical way to maintain peace. Moreover, the destruction of this illusion must be largely blamed on aggressive countries such as Italy, Germany, and Japan. Now Mussolini is killing the patient with a knife in one hand, and telling people that the patient was going to die anyway, blaming the doctor who treated him for being meddlesome. This is really illogical.

Due to Mussolini's attack on the "illusion" of peace, he will naturally oppose France and the Soviet Union, because France and the Soviet Union are the strongest supporters of collective peace and the League of Nations. Mussolini said that the relationship between France and Italy after the Rome Agreement was very close, but since France insisted on the League of Nations' sanctions against Italy, it had to take retaliatory measures. And for the communism of the Soviet Union, Mussolini now wants to resume his initial opposition movement. This clearly shows the result of the Italo-German talks: Italy is taking a more pro-German, anti-French, and anti-Soviet policy.

Secondly, regarding the countries in the Danube River basin, Austria and Hungary have been under the influence of Rome since the establishment of the Three-Power Protocol. However, Mussolini's special support for Hungary's revision of the peace treaty, the recovery of lost territories, and the satisfaction in the near future is a clear expression, which is rare in the past and a direct attack on the countries of the Little Entente. No wonder it has caused great repercussions in Romania and Czechoslovakia. But the most strange thing is the relationship between Italy and Yugoslavia. Mussolini indicated that there is a possibility of improvement. We all know that the conflict between Italy, Yugoslavia, Hungary, and Yugoslavia has been very serious in the past ten years. But now Mussolini says that a friendly relationship can be established. This clearly shows that Mussolini wants to win over Yugoslavia and break up the unity of the Little Entente. Because Yugoslavia has always been strongly opposed to communism and has not yet recognized the Soviet Union, it is inevitable that it will arouse Italy's delusions. Italy's aggressive policy towards the Danube countries will inevitably increase the disputes in the Central European political situation.

Again, Italy's policy towards Britain may undergo major changes in the future. Since the East African War, the severity of the conflict between Britain and Italy is known to everyone. But in Mussolini's speech, although he firmly stated that if Britain does not respect Italy's interests and status in the Mediterranean, then Italy will not hesitate to go to war, in his heart, Mussolini revealed the intention of compromise with Britain. Therefore, The Times said, "Britain is very encouraged by Mussolini's eagerness to improve relations between Britain and Italy." And the Daily Mail said, "Britain should immediately respond to Mussolini's frankness and expressions of goodwill." Other newspapers also have similar criticisms. From this, it can be seen that Italy's policy towards Britain will undergo great changes in the future. The main reason for the change is the result of the Italo-German talks, because Germany wants to win over Britain in order to deal with the peace front, so that it will not lean towards France and the Soviet Union. The recent German-Italian approval of calling the Locarno Conference earlier is a side proof.

Mussolini's speech involved all the important issues in Europe, but he did not say a word about the most serious Spanish war. This is very noteworthy. Perhaps the talks between Germany and Italy have not yet reached a compromise on this matter. However, based on our analysis of Mussolini's speech, we can already determine that the relationship between Italy and Germany has become closer than before, and the unity of the Fascist front has also developed further than before. This threat to peace in Europe and the world is, of course, very serious.

British Parliament Reconvenes; King's Speech Emphasizes the Far East; Hopes for Successful Sino-Japanese Negotiations; Foreign Policy Based on the League of Nations. 49

(London) The new session of Parliament held its official opening ceremony today. The King's speech expressed the hope to revisit India after the coronation and mentioned that the British government is concerned about the political situation in the Far East and hopes that the current Sino-Japanese negotiations will achieve satisfactory results. His Majesty originally planned to travel from Buckingham Palace to Westminster in the carriage used by the late King George V during his coronation, but it was canceled due to rain and changed to a car. The escort was the Duke of Beaufort, the Grand Chamberlain of the Inner Court. This morning, it rained heavily, and since there was no sign of improvement, the original plan was changed. However, the crowd watching along the road was still very crowded, and the road was full of umbrellas. The relentless rain and thin fog made the surroundings gray, but the people's enthusiasm for welcoming was not diminished. Cheers erupted as the car passed by. Inside the House of Lords, the ceremony was held as usual. Since His Majesty has not yet been crowned, he did not wear the imperial crown. Queen Mother Mary's cold has gradually healed, but she has not yet left her room, so she did not attend. Only the King's three younger brothers participated in the ceremony. The King first made a solemn Christian oath, and then read the speech, which mainly stated that the British government's policy is still based on the League of Nations member states, so it will strive to promote the conference of the five countries of the Locarno Pact. The Imperial Conference to be held in London in May next year will provide the representatives of the imperial governments with the opportunity to discuss and re-prove the value of enhancing close understanding. When the coronation ceremony is held, he hopes to visit India again, so that the princes and people of that place will know that he has inherited the imperial crown. Strengthening the defense plan is essential for the protection of the empire, and the government is very satisfied with this. The British government is also concerned about the political situation in the Far East, and peace and tranquility there are closely related to the interests of the British people in that part of the world, so it sincerely hopes that the current Sino-Japanese negotiations will achieve a satisfactory solution. British industry and commerce now have the hope of continuing to develop. The government is now considering a merchant shipping maintenance plan suitable for the needs of the country, and indicates the legal system for reorganizing the coal mining industry and dealing with individuals and the state who disturb public order, but without hindering their legitimate freedom of speech or assembly. The government also intends to propose bills for the development of domestic agriculture and fisheries within the Factory Law, and will use a great plan to improve the national physique, especially focusing on young people. (Reuters, 3rd)

Regarding Mussolini's Speech, Britain Expresses Willingness to Accept, but on the Premise of a New Locarno Pact; Hopes for Mutual Respect for Mediterranean Rights. 50

(London) Officials believe that Mussolini's speech in Milan yesterday, regarding the conclusion of a Mediterranean agreement, requires the establishment of a new Locarno Pact before this agreement can be concluded. The British public also believes that most of Mussolini's speech is practical common sense, so before proceeding with negotiations on the Mediterranean issue, negotiations on a new Locarno Pact must be started first. Moreover, if this Mediterranean agreement is to be negotiated, it may immediately cause problems for various countries in the eastern Mediterranean, and the Spanish incident is also difficult to avoid being involved. Britain has solemnly declared that the method of recognizing Italy's conquest of Abyssinia, as requested by Mussolini, is difficult to implement at present, but the British government has recognized Italy's power in Abyssinia as a fait accompli, because the British Embassy in Abyssinia has already established relations with the Italian Governor-General of Abyssinia, Graziani. Britain's only concern about the Mediterranean is the maintenance of the status quo. Britain has long expressed its willingness to recognize Italy's interests in the Mediterranean, but Italy must also respect Britain's interests there. In short, from the British point of view, the new Locarno Pact is the most useful step to resolve the European situation. (Reuters, 2nd)

France Continues to Support the League of Nations; Says It Is Not Completely Hopeless Regarding the Disarmament Issue. 51

(Paris) The Foreign Ministry spokesperson reiterated today France's support for the League of Nations and the collective security proposition, saying that France still hopes to maintain world peace and implement disarmament. We are not completely hopeless that countries around the world will reconsider the issue of disarmament. (National Telegraph, 2nd)

This refers to the visit of Admiral Horthy. (Havas, 2nd)

I also respectfully express my friendship to you." Well-informed sources also said that the Italian Prime Minister had already decided on his attitude towards the Central European issue several years ago, and the speech he made today is only a natural result. (Havas, 2nd)

Spanish Rebels Bomb the Vicinity of Madrid Airport; Planes Attack the Capital Twice; Non-Intervention Committee Meets Again. 54

(Lisbon) According to the Spanish rebel army, the attack on Madrid has made significant progress. It has occupied Villaviciosa, ten miles southwest of the capital, and has advanced along the Aranjuez-Madrid Avenue to within three miles of the tram terminus on the outskirts of the capital. At dawn this morning, the Nationalist army began shelling the Getafe air force base, nine miles south of the capital, and will then attack with infantry. It is expected that Getafe can fall within a few hours. The Nationalist army north of the capital is now crossing the Guadarrama Mountains and the Leon Pass, advancing towards Villalba. If the Nationalist army occupies the town, the position of the Escorial government army will be seriously threatened. (Reuters, 3rd)

(Navalcarnero) A special dispatch from our reporter stated that the Nationalist army advanced yesterday along the highway between this city and Madrid, and occupied the two towns of Villamantilla and Villanueva Canada. Until 5:00 p.m., it fought fiercely with the government army again, defeated it, and occupied the town of Brunete. From now on, the Nationalist army's positions between Navalcarnero and Chapineria have become one. In this battle, 300 members of the government army were killed, including many Russians. (Havas, 3rd)

(Madrid) Rebel planes attacked here twice today, once at 9:00 a.m. and once at 5:00 p.m. In the first attack, three men, two women, and three children died in the suburbs of the capital. (Reuters, 2nd)

(Madrid) Several Nationalist army planes flew over Valdeiglesias, near the suburbs, this morning and dropped bombs, killing three children and injuring seven others. (Havas, 2nd)

(London) The Sub-Committee established by the Adjustment Committee for the Spanish Civil War Non-Intervention Method met at 3:30 p.m. today and ended at 7:00 p.m. According to the suggestion put forward by Lord Plymouth, the chairman of the Adjustment Committee and the British Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs (referring to monitoring the Spanish seaports and the border between Portugal and Spain), it discussed how to enhance the monitoring method of non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War. The representatives of the countries agreed to request instructions from their respective governments. The Sub-Committee then discussed the suggestion put forward by the Soviet representative to monitor the Portuguese seaports. The representatives of the major countries successively expressed their opposition, and said that the border between Portugal and Spain should implement the monitoring method, so there is no need to monitor the Portuguese seaports. The Soviet representative refuted this view, saying that if the Portuguese seaports can be monitored, then the situation of shipping weapons to Spain by plane will no longer occur. As a result, the Sub-Committee did not make a decision and adjourned. It will continue to be discussed at the next meeting or at the plenary meeting of the Adjustment Committee on the 4th of this month. The date of the next meeting of the Sub-Committee has not yet been decided. As for the plenary meeting of the Adjustment Committee, if the representatives of the countries have received instructions from their respective governments by then, the issue of monitoring the Portuguese seaports can be submitted for discussion, but it is feared that the instructions will be difficult to send by then. (Havas, 2nd)

Japan's 2 Million Reserve Soldiers Hold a Conference. 55

(Tokyo) 3 million army and navy reserve soldiers nationwide held a ceremony on the 3rd of the Meiji Festival to commemorate the 26th anniversary of the founding and the promulgation of the new association order. This was the cabinet meeting on September 18th, and in accordance with the great policy of streamlining the military, the ordinance was formulated to transform the private organization into a powerful state organization. Therefore, the ceremony on this day was very grand and solemn. At 1:00 p.m., 1,850 members of each branch, wearing army and navy uniforms, gathered at the auditorium of the Kudan Military Hall. At 2:00 p.m., officials such as Army Minister Terauchi, Navy Minister Nagano, Rural Military Association President Suzuki, and Vice President Nakano lined up at the front gate to respectfully welcome His Highness Prince Kan'in, the president. At 3:00 p.m., at the Grand Auditorium of the hall, under the presence of the President, they respectfully recited the President's will, and the guests from the army and navy delivered congratulatory speeches, sang the Rural Military Association song, and shouted "Long live His Majesty the Great Commander" three times. The ceremony ended at 4:00 p.m. His Majesty the Great Commander bestowed a generous imperial edict at midnight. (Domei, 3rd)

Fukushima Earthquake Affects Kanto Too 56

Fukushima: An earthquake occurred here at 5:45 AM this morning, startling citizens from their sleep and causing them to flee outdoors, leading to temporary chaos. The extent of the damage is still being investigated, but when the earthquake struck, roof tiles flew, shop windows shattered, and electricity and telephone lines were cut, completely disrupting long-distance communication. However, it appears that neither people nor livestock were harmed. According to the Fukushima Observatory, the earthquake occurred at 5:46:26.5 AM on the 3rd, with an initial tremor lasting 16 seconds, a seismic intensity of 1.2 millimeters, an epicenter located 120 kilometers northeast of Kin-Hua Mountain off the coast of Fukushima Prefecture, a total duration of 10 minutes, and a moderate nature, not significantly different from previous earthquakes in the Sanriku region. (3rd, DOMEI News)

(Tokyo) At 5:46 AM this morning, a strong earthquake struck the Kanto region, with tremors felt over a wide area, including the Tohoku region, the entire Kanto region, and parts of the Chubu region. The tremors were most severe in Fukushima, Miyagi, and Iwate. The epicenter was in the deep sea northeast of Fukushima, resulting in relatively little damage. Had the epicenter been on land, it would have been a major earthquake, causing a terrible disaster. (3rd, DOMEI News)

Four Thousand Several Hundred Million Voters Decide the American Political Situation: Presidential Election Held Yesterday; Various Parties Predict Roosevelt's Advantage 57

(New York) The people who are preparing to vote for the president tomorrow number a total of 45 million. The success or failure of the Democratic candidate, President Roosevelt, and the Republican candidate, Governor Landon, rests in the hands of these individuals. Election Day is a national holiday. Clubs, bars, and restaurants are all busy preparing, but until the polling places close, no beer or alcohol of any kind may be sold. Movie theaters nationwide are finding ways to project election results on the screen. It is feared that more than 100,000 citizens will gather in Times Square in New York, waiting for the various colored lights from the top of the tower to indicate the election situation. Radio stations will report the results at any time, without stopping all day long. The Associated Press has already leased 280,000 miles of telegraph lines, ready to send telegrams reporting election vote counts at any time, and will employ 50,000 personnel to count the votes. The police are preparing for possible riots in eastern New York and will station strong police forces there as a precaution. Many businesses on New York's Heng Street have announced that they will remain open all night during the election to report the news to their London branches. (2nd, Reuters News)

(New York) Before the election, various parties are still making efforts to study the results of "mock voting." Only the Literary Digest and Hua Weekly predict Landon will win. According to the results of the mock voting held by the New York Newsletter, Roosevelt won by a large margin, with 315 electoral votes, exceeding the 266 votes required for the election. The New York Times announced that Roosevelt has 236 votes that can be determined and 170 votes that are promising. It is not yet known whether the Pacific Coast Seamen's Strike will have an impact on the election. American media tycoon Hearst arrived here yesterday from Europe aboard the Queen Mary. According to his prediction, Landon should be able to win. The New York Evening Journal, which he runs, published an editorial urging readers to vote for Landon to save America. (2nd, Reuters News)

(New York) Today, the banking community is betting on President Roosevelt's victory in this election by a ratio of five to two. Last Saturday night, the ratio was eight to five. As for the situation in various states, Roosevelt also has the lead, with a ratio of two to one in New York, six to five in Ohio, three to two in Illinois, and four to one in California. Landon has the lead in New Jersey, with a ratio of seven to five. In Pennsylvania, Roosevelt and Landon are evenly matched, both with a ratio of three to two. (2nd, National News)

American Voters Vote in the Rain: The Tendency of the Middle Class is Unclear; Landon Takes the Lead in the First Few Places 58

(New York) This morning, the sky was gloomy and there was rain. The American people went to the polling places to elect the president. Twelve voters from the village of Millsfield, New Hampshire, went to vote one minute before midnight, hoping to gain the honor of being the first to vote. Of these twelve people, five voted for Landon, two voted for President Roosevelt, and the remaining five abstained temporarily. Many places in the United States are betting that President Roosevelt will not win, but the tendency of the middle class is still a mystery and may suddenly change dramatically. It is expected that President Roosevelt will win a majority of the votes from the labor community, the unemployed, and young people, but the middle class is frightened by propaganda, and it is not known to what extent. Whether the intense propaganda against the New Deal has an impact on the "white-collar" class can only be proven by voting today. All the votes cast in the village of Somerset, Vermont, were for Landon. According to the first report from Houston Town, Texas, President Roosevelt currently has 126 votes and Landon has 21 votes. (3rd, Reuters News)

The results of the election in the village of Millsfield, New Haven, show that Republican candidate Landon won. The entire village had a total of twelve voters. Voting began at midnight and ended immediately after seven votes were cast. Landon received five votes. This village is the first in the United States to report the election results. (2nd, National News Agency)

Massachusetts, New Ashford: As a result of the election in this town, Republican presidential candidate Landon received 26 votes, and President Roosevelt received 19 votes. This is the first fully disclosed result in the country. In the town of Tolland, Maine, Landon received 44 votes, and Roosevelt received 21 votes. (3rd, National News Agency)

Topeka: Republican presidential candidate Landon and his wife went to vote at midnight today. (2nd, National News)

(Washington) The Meteorological Bureau predicted today that voters will encounter rain, snow, and severe cold tomorrow. Sunshine is expected in West Michigan, Florida, and the Carolinas. Snow will fall in Illinois, Indiana, Missouri, Michigan, Wisconsin, Iowa, and parts of Kansas. Heavy rain will fall in New York. The Atlantic coastal states of Massachusetts, Virginia, Alabama, Arkansas, Georgia, Louisiana, Kentucky, and West Virginia will experience rain and a cold wave is approaching the Midwest. (2nd, National News)

Election Analysis 59

(New York) President Roosevelt and Republican presidential candidate Landon will both broadcast "fireside chats" on the radio tonight, ending the most expensive campaign in history. Voting will begin tomorrow morning. According to today's gambling in various cities, everyone is betting on Roosevelt's election. The total cost of this campaign exceeded 13 million yuan, of which 7 million yuan was spent by the Republican Party, 4 million yuan by the Democratic Party, and the rest by smaller organizations such as the Liberty League, the National Social Justice League, and the United Mine Workers. Democratic National Committee Chairman Farley said that President Roosevelt can get the support of 46 states, with only Maine and Vermont electing Landon. Republican National Committee Chairman Hamilton believes that Landon has a good chance, saying that the 14 states east of the Mississippi River and north of the Ohio River will elect Landon, and that he is confident even in the far western states. As for the congressional elections, Republicans expect to gain 45 seats in the House of Representatives. Democrats privately admit that they will lose about 35 seats. However, although Republicans may slightly increase their seats in the Senate, even if Landon is elected, he will not be able to seize control. Statisticians estimate today that between 42 million and 45 million voters will vote. Observers believe that during the campaign, the model of a new party has been formed. All left-wing and radical elements will vote for the Democratic Party, while conservative Democrats will switch to the Republican Party, and there are quite a few fence-sitters, such as Senators Johnson and Borah, who have not said a word. (2nd, National News)

(New York) The 48 states of the United States are scheduled to hold general elections and congressional elections tomorrow. Between 42 million and 45 million voters will participate in the voting. They will elect (1) 531 election representatives, that is, one representative is elected for every 279,712 citizens; (2) 467 members of Congress, that is, 435 members of the House of Representatives and one-third of the senators, totaling 32; and (3) 33 governors. According to the American general election, a two-stage election system is used. First, voters in each state elect "election representatives," which is the primary election. Then, the election representatives will elect a president and vice president each in the state capitals on December 14 of this year, which is the second election. During the primary election, if a political party can win a majority of the votes in a state, then all the election representatives in that state will belong to that party. For example, the state of New York has a total of 10 million voters. If Party A gets only ten more votes than Party B, then all 47 election representatives in that state will belong to Party A. This determines the general election. The parties participating in the competition include the Democratic Party, the Republican Party, the Socialist Party, and the Communist Party. Among them, the Socialist and Communist parties have very little power and are not worth mentioning. Therefore, the situation of this competition should be the same as in previous elections. In other words, it is a contest between the Democratic candidate, President Roosevelt, and the Republican candidate, Kansas Governor Landon. As for the campaign speeches delivered by President Roosevelt and Governor Landon, most of them are about domestic issues, and rarely mention foreign policy. Only once did Landon criticize the current government's foreign trade policy, that is, the reciprocal trade agreements established between the United States and various countries. Later, Secretary of State Hull and Secretary of the Interior Ickes successively responded, saying that the reciprocal trade agreements would not only be maintained, but that similar agreements should also be signed with other countries in the future. If we speculate on the election results, both the Democratic and Republican parties claim to be confident of victory. According to the New York Times, the election situation in the major states is still uncertain, among which the state of New York is the most important (the state of New York will elect as many as 47 election representatives). The states of Pennsylvania, Illinois, Ohio, and Texas are decisive. If the Republican Party can win in these four states, then Landon has a chance of being elected. In short, President Roosevelt's hope of being elected is the strongest. Also, during tomorrow's election, most places will still have voters fill out election ballots and put them in ballot boxes, and then count them, as in the past. However, in major cities, such as New York City, special machines will be used to automatically calculate the votes in order to make it more convenient. This is also a feature of this election. (2nd, Havas News)

Roosevelt and Landon Deliver Final Campaign Speeches: Both are Concerned about Freedom and Democracy 60

(New York) Tomorrow is the date of the primary election. Democratic candidate President Roosevelt and Republican candidate Kansas Governor Landon both delivered radio speeches on the evening of this day, about fifteen minutes each, to end the campaign. President Roosevelt delivered his speech at his hometown of Hyde Park, New York (the Roosevelt family has voted there in every election for more than a hundred years). He said, "There is a trend in some parts of the world that threatens to engulf democratic systems, but in our America, people still believe in democracy as before and have not been moved by it. The majority rules the minority, which is the law recognized by the United States. We firmly uphold the traditional ideas and experiences of the United States for our own reasons. The election is tomorrow, and when you vote, you must put aside thoughts of gratitude and grievances, and promote the prosperity and welfare of the United States as the only goal. Governor Landon's speech was delivered at his private residence in Topeka, the capital of Kansas. He said, "The nation will accept a major responsibility tomorrow. The situation is such that there is a need to form a free and democratic line in the world, and we must uphold this line, which is our inescapable responsibility." (2nd, Havas News)

Hyde Park: President Roosevelt addressed American voters in his famous "fireside chat" tonight to end his election campaign, warning voters not to act against their conscience and be afraid when voting tomorrow, saying, "Whoever is elected tomorrow will ultimately be the president of all the people, so it is appropriate not to be afraid of electing the person you consider perfect in your mind. Moreover, the election is a personal matter, and others can never blame you for not choosing what they want. We are all equal before the ballot box." Roosevelt also praised the open methods of the opposition party, saying that the people can understand the current points of contention, which is very beneficial to the democratic system. The American citizens of 1936 are the products of a free system, and I am not afraid of the threats of politicians or the ambitions of dictators, because they can hardly use their skills for long in nations with freedom of thought and freedom of action. (2nd, National News Agency)

Topeka: Republican presidential candidate Landon delivered his last speech here tonight on the eve of the general election, saying, "When you vote tomorrow, you should vote as Americans for the future of Americans. We must strictly adhere to the line of democracy and dare not slacken. When you vote tomorrow, you should be determined to uphold the three principles on which the American people rely to be great, namely, love of freedom, enthusiasm for justice, and humanitarian habits." This speech was broadcast nationally by the radio station in Topeka, the capital of Kansas. (2nd, National News Agency)

American Seamen's Strike: Claiming Communist Agitation; Number of Strikers Increases to 100,000; Government May Take Strong Measures 61

(New York) The seamen's strike is expanding, and it is said that communists are instigating it. The Seamen's Union here announced today that 133 ships are currently out of service on the Atlantic coast. About 10,000 seamen are striking on the Atlantic and Gulf coasts. Most ships from Europe will also be out of service after arriving here in the future. The mail ship Manhattan and the Virginia have canceled their schedules, so 21 ships here have stopped. The Seamen's Union held a secret meeting today. International Seamen's Union Director Crum stated that if the shipowners request assistance from the Navy and Customs Enforcement, the union will announce a general strike. (2nd, National News)

(New York) Third Vice President Grange of the International Seamen's Union issued a statement today, strongly criticizing the current shipping strike as an illegal movement organized by the Communist Party. He has planned to supply sailors to the ships that are out of service so that the strike cannot last long. This dispute is a struggle between communism and Americanism. At the same time, the San Francisco Seamen's Union has ordered the strike to be extended to all parts of the country. (3rd, Reuters News)

Philadelphia: Philadelphia Mayor Wilson announced today that the national seamen's strike is illegal, and ten pickets have been arrested and imprisoned. (2nd, National News)

(San Francisco) The strike on the Pacific coast has now spread to related industries. By Wednesday, 100,000 people will be out of work, so the government may take "strong measures" to stop it. Labor Secretary McGrady, who was ordered to come here to preside over labor-management negotiations, said today that the seamen's strike is a challenge to national welfare, and announced that the capitalists intend to ask the Navy to provide "safe crew members" to protect perishable goods, and said, "Now water transportation has been blocked, which will directly and indirectly affect the lives of the people across the country. The government must crack down on any organization, labor or management, whose actions endanger national welfare in order to protect the country and the people." Today, the capitalists initially decided to express their willingness not to strike, but to operate the ships on their own. Although there is no such plan at present, it is believed that ships must be protected from fire and other dangers. This confirms the saying that the capitalists may order a small number of sailors to board the ships. The suspension of shipping has spread to the Atlantic coast and the ports of the Gulf of Mexico. Eighteen ships are holding sympathy strikes in the port of New York, and another fifty-nine ships are holding strikes in other ports on the Atlantic coast. The total number of strikers reaches more than 5,000. More than 5,000 people are also striking in the Gulf of Mexico. (2nd, National News Agency)

(New York) The labor unrest has now spread to the Atlantic coast and the ports of the Gulf of Mexico, threatening the entire American shipping industry. The Shipping Committee is conducting a thorough investigation in San Francisco today to try to break the deadlock, but the representatives of the Pacific branch of the Seamen's Union angrily left the meeting, saying that they opposed the investigation and refused to submit the case. However, the committee continued to listen to the report and did not stop because of their withdrawal. The American largest airship Virginia, which was scheduled to sail to the Pacific coast tomorrow, has canceled due to the seamen's strike, and the 500 passengers on board have disembarked and returned home. The ship is the 19th ship affected by the strike. The American Steamship Owners Association has convened a meeting of American shipping leaders to consider the overall situation. Several ports, such as Philadelphia and Boston, have successively held strikes. In Boston, the crew of the engine room of the mail ship New York completely left the ship a few minutes before departure, preventing it from departing. The 300 passengers on board were sent to New York by train. The situation in the port of New York is very quiet. No pickets are stationed at the wharf, and the dispatched police have nothing to do. The International Seamen's Union announced that the shipowners have agreed to increase wages by an average of 20% in the ports between Wilmington, North Carolina, and Tampa, Florida. The shipowners took this action because there are also signs of a strike in the Southeast. The mail ship Manhattan, which was scheduled to sail to Europe on Wednesday, has canceled its schedule due to the seamen's strike, and the ship fares paid by the 350 passengers have been refunded. (2nd, Reuters News)

(New York) The International Seamen's Union here immediately announced a slowdown in support, causing 20,000 seamen on the Atlantic and Gulf coasts to stop working, resulting in 107 ships being unable to sail, including as many as 26 ships anchored in the port of New York. (2nd, Havas News)

Honolulu: All ships in this port have announced a strike in sympathy with the American shipping strike. It is heard that some travelers traveling around the world are stranded here as a result, including two American consuls to China. Due to the suspension of ships, the mail volume of the Clipper flying boat across the Pacific has surged. (2nd, Reuters News)

According to the company's general director, Norman, British wireless cinema broadcasting is more advanced than any other country. When the coronation ceremony is held next year, people elsewhere may be able to see and hear the grand occasion. (2nd, Reuters News)

Chaozhou-Shantou People Appeal for Reduction and Exemption of Harsh Taxes and Miscellaneous Levies; Local Areas Arbitrarily Impose Taxes, Resulting in Multiple Taxes on a Single Item; Marriage of Daughters Requires Tax Payment, Otherwise Considered Abduction; Various Harsh and Miscellaneous Levies Emerge Endlessly 64

Shantou Correspondence: After the renewal of the Guangdong administration, the government immediately implemented the abolition of harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies to alleviate the people's suffering. However, in the Chaozhou and Meizhou counties, there are numerous types of harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies, and the amount collected and its usage are largely unclear. The collectors of these taxes and levies are mostly county councils, district and township offices, guard teams, police districts, autonomous offices, schools, local public organizations, party headquarters, and other institutions. Currently, the county councils and party headquarters have ceased operations, and district and township autonomous organizations have also been suspended. The guard teams will be downsized into security forces, and police districts will remain as before. Various harsh and miscellaneous taxes, such as land tax surcharges, should be reduced. However, the counties still maintain countless taxes, leading to indescribable suffering for the people. The item of rice alone is subject to multiple taxes. On the 26th, the Shantou Chamber of Commerce, the North-South Trade Association, and others sent a special telegram to the Ministry of Finance, requesting the prior exemption of special taxes on imported rice to alleviate the people's food shortage. The original telegram stated, "Upon investigation, domestic rice has been snatched up by Japanese merchants everywhere, resulting in empty stocks and skyrocketing prices. Currently, there is little rice stored in Chaozhou and Meizhou, and coupled with the disaster of drought and locusts, the autumn harvest is worrisome. The price of rice has risen from six yuan to ten yuan per dan (a unit of weight), causing widespread panic. If no replenishment is made in advance, there is no way to stabilize the people's hearts. We humbly request that the import of foreign rice into Chaozhou and Meizhou be temporarily exempted from special taxes, so that it can be purchased and imported to stabilize prices and alleviate the famine." Furthermore, various public associations in Chaoyang County and other counties telegraphed the provincial government to abolish harsh levies and surcharges, stating, "The Guangdong government is corrupt, and incompetent and greedy officials fill the political arena, colluding with each other. For years, they have been imposing excessive taxes and levies, with hundreds of tax items emerging, making it impossible for the people to survive. Leaving aside provincial and national taxes, various local taxes and levies are such that almost every item is taxed multiple times, with unbearable harshness and complexity. The organizers claim the levies are for autonomous expenses, relief funds, or security needs, creating clever names and arbitrarily imposing taxes, draining the people's resources and causing the collapse of all industries, akin to exhausting the pond to catch all the fish. The strong are driven to take risks, while the weak are left to fill the ditches. Public resentment is boiling, and cries of anguish fill the air. Our association and others find it difficult to remain silent, and after the fifth board meeting, it was resolved to list the names of various taxes and levies that should be abolished and submit them to the Guangdong Provincial Committee for the Abolition of Harsh Taxes and Miscellaneous Levies, requesting a review and abolition to alleviate the people's suffering." According to investigations, in addition to legitimate taxes and levies, each county has over a hundred types of harsh and miscellaneous levies, and each district and township has over twenty types. For example, in rural villages, when a woman gets married, there are so-called "daughter's departure tax," "new bride flower tax," "marriage certificate tax," "district office certificate stamp fee," "dowry tax," "face powder tax," "ceremonial guard tax," "drum and music tax," "wedding banquet tax," "matchmaker commission tax," and "auspicious and inauspicious occasions tax." Not only are wealthy families afraid to formally marry under the weight of these overlapping harsh levies, but poor families also lack the qualifications to enjoy the joy of a new marriage. For example, if a rural woman formally marries through a matchmaker, the bride price is eighty yuan. When the matchmaker delivers the ancestral records, they must register with the district office and obtain a marriage certificate, costing four yuan, plus a four-cent stamp. The matchmaker and an additional matchmaker receive eight yuan, plus an additional eight yuan for the matchmaker's commission, with the bride's and groom's families each contributing four yuan. Otherwise, the matchmaker's qualifications will be revoked, and the marriage will not be considered a formal marriage with proper betrothal gifts. Furthermore, before setting the auspicious day, a departure tax of four yuan must be paid before the bride can leave the house, otherwise, it will be considered abduction. When the woman boards the bridal sedan chair, the sedan chair carriers must first pay the tax to the tax bureau before they can carry the sedan chair to the bride's home; otherwise, it will be considered smuggling and tax evasion, and the sedan chair shop and carriers will be punished and disqualified from their profession. The sedan chair tax ranges from two to four yuan per chair. Unless the bride walks on foot, she cannot avoid paying this tax. However, according to village customs, walking on foot is not allowed in the village. If the new bride has a clothing chest with her, it is called the dowry tax, which is charged at two to four cents per load. Wealthy people who marry off their daughters may be charged dozens of yuan. If there are drums, music, and ceremonial guards in front of the bride's sedan chair, there are additional taxes, costing one yuan per set, with a double charge for those with gongs. The tax for auspicious and inauspicious occasions is for the purpose of settling wandering vagrants and beggars. The family hosting the wedding must pay over ten or twenty yuan to avoid the misery of disturbance at the door. Relatives who come to congratulate bring wedding banquets, and the kitchen dishes are assessed by the banquet tax inspector. Those with shark fin, abalone, and sea cucumber are charged an additional two percent, while those with pork, chicken, and fish are charged an additional one percent. Each table of food costs at least one yuan in tax, and the chefs and restaurant owners are responsible. If one prepares the banquet oneself, one must first notify the tax bureau for inspection. In short, those who know even a little about the suffering caused by harsh levies to the people of Chaozhou and Meizhou cannot help but stick out their tongues in dismay. For example, many farming families rely on raising pigs as a sideline. From the time the boar is used for breeding, there are the following taxes: "breeding tax," "piglet tax," "piglet bar tax" (when piglets are sold), "weighing commission tax," "big pig tax," "pig manure boat tax," "slaughter tax," "meat stall tax," "health inspection tax" (failure to inspect will be considered inflating the pigs), "pig bristle tax," "pig oil export tax," and "banquet tax." Even after being eaten and turned into feces, one must still pay the "feces and urine tax" to the collective agricultural company. Therefore, it is no wonder that the people of Chaozhou and Shantou are calling for tax reductions and lighter levies.

During the Japanese Army's Grand Maneuvers, a Banquet at Huai Ren Hall; Tashiro Kan'ichiro Attends Inspection; Song Zheyuan Hosts a Grand Banquet, Frankly Discussing Sincere Cooperation; The Evening Concludes with Chinese and Western Songs 65

Beiping Correspondence: The North China Garrison Army of Japan held its autumn grand maneuvers. The 2nd was the eighth day, and all Japanese soldiers were concentrated in Tong County for rest. All schools, hotels, theaters, and other places were full of Japanese soldiers. Many students of the Tong County Normal School came from other places. The school was occupied, so the local authorities gave each student two yuan to find their own place to live, and they would return to school after the maneuvers were over. The Japanese Army Headquarters was located in the special agency in the rice warehouse. Tashiro Kan'ichiro, the commander, arrived in Peiping by express train from Tianjin on the afternoon of the 2nd. The scene at the station was not as serious as last time. In addition to several dozen Chinese and Japanese welcomers, including Qin Dechun, Chen Juesheng, Chen Zhongfu, Chen Jiyan, Matsumuro, Kato, and Kuwabara, there were no Japanese soldiers guarding the station. After getting off the train, Tashiro went to the Fusang Hall to rest briefly, and then went to Huai Ren Hall in Zhongnanhai at 12:30 to attend the banquet hosted by Song Zheyuan. After the banquet, he took a car to Tong County. At about 3:00, he summoned Hashimoto and other responsible persons such as Shinagawa to the headquarters to inquire in detail about the locations of the maneuvering troops and all preparations for the general maneuvers on the 3rd.

When Song held a banquet for Tashiro at Huai Ren Hall, he also invited important figures from all walks of life and various institutions to accompany them. The Japanese attendees included Tashiro, Matsumuro, Imamura, Hamada, Imai, Nakajima, Sakurai, Satani, Yamamine, Nishida, Matsuo, Kuwabara, Kato, Akato, and Hirai. The Chinese attendees included the host Song Zheyuan, as well as Qi Xieyuan, Jia Deyao, Qin Dechun, Jiang Menglin, Li Zheng, Xu Songming, Li Linyu, Zhou Jingwen, Qi Dapeng, Men Zhizhong, Tang Erhe, Deng Zhexi, Shi Yousan, Hu Yukun, Chen Zhongfu, Chen Juesheng, Niu Chuanshan, Leng Jiaji, Zhang Shizhao, Liu Chunlin, Liu Zhizhou, Lu Zongyu, Zhu Shen, Li Mingzhong, Liu Yufen, Pan Yugui, Guo Zhihan, Ge Dingyuan, Lei Sishang, Wang Xicheng, Yue Qianzhai, Zou Quansun, Fu Zhankui, Sun Weihao, Zhang Weifan, Shao Wenkai, Chen Jiyan, Lin Shize, Wang Lengzhai, Guan Yixian and others, totaling more than eighty people. The meal was Chinese food. After taking their seats, Song stood up and delivered a speech, which was translated by Chen Zhongfu, chairman of the Foreign Affairs Committee. His speech stated, "Today, Commander Tashiro has arrived in Peiping. I would like to take this opportunity to prepare a simple meal and wine to show my respect as the host, and to invite Chinese and Japanese people to accompany us, to have a friendly gathering and introduce each other. China and Japan are two major Asian nations and brotherly countries, sharing common interests. China has a vast territory and abundant resources, but its development is backward, which is the focus of world attention. Japan has a strong national power and rapid development, which is also the focus of world attention. Both countries are struggling and striving in the world, and it is natural for them to coexist and prosper. Sincere cooperation based on equality between the two countries is a common understanding among people with insight in both countries, and there is no need to elaborate. The Hebei-Chahar Political Council has been established for a year, and we have been working towards this goal, advocating peace internally and externally, opposing communist riots, and maintaining social order with sincerity and fairness in order to achieve progress. However, there have been doubts in society over the past year. The first doubt is that Japan is invading North China, and the second doubt is that the North China authorities have any secrets with the Japanese side. Regarding the first point, the Japanese authorities have repeatedly and solemnly stated that they have no intention of invading North China's land and sovereignty. Regarding the second point, since the establishment of this political council, North China has had no secrets with Japan. The opening of transportation, postal services, and navigation are all continuations of previous unfinished negotiations. We are seeking to achieve the goal of sincere cooperation based on the principle of equality and mutual benefit. I would like to sincerely state this during this toast with Commander Tashiro, so that it may be known and believed by all parties."

After Song finished his speech, he raised his glass to Tashiro to propose a toast, and everyone applauded. Tashiro stood up in the applause to deliver a reply, which was also translated by Chen Zhongfu. He stated, "I have come to Peiping for the autumn maneuvers, and I would like to take this opportunity to accept Chairman Song's invitation to a banquet and to meet leaders from all walks of life. I am deeply honored. I would also like to express my gratitude to Chairman Song and all aspects of your country for providing various conveniences for the autumn maneuvers. The houses and all utensils needed during the maneuvers were all helped by the Chinese people. This further demonstrates that Chairman Song and the Chinese people deeply understand the friendship and relations between China and Japan. Therefore, I would like to express my deep gratitude. The points Chairman Song mentioned regarding the relationship between China and Japan are generally consistent with my feelings. Chairman Song said that China and Japan should cooperate sincerely based on the principle of equality and mutual benefit. This is extremely pertinent. I admire Chairman Song's patriotic and caring zeal. In the past, there have inevitably been imperfections in the relationship between the two societies, which have led to misunderstandings, and there have always been people who intentionally slander. In my opinion, facts speak louder than words, and in the end, they are not worth the laughter of those in the know. I have several things that can prove this. First, when I first arrived in Tianjin to take office, there were rumors that Japan had some kind of action against Hebei and Chahar. Now that much time has passed, there is complete factual evidence to show that these rumors have been completely shattered. Second, when the Fengtai incident occurred, someone deliberately spread rumors, but it was finally resolved due to mutual understanding. This is another example not worth laughing at. Third, with this Japanese autumn maneuvers, there are rumors that Japan wants to take this opportunity to take action. Newspapers everywhere have records of this. Now, what is the reality? The outside world should already be fully aware. In short, misunderstandings are ultimately misunderstandings, and rumors are ultimately rumors. The events of the three eastern provinces will never be seen in Hebei and Chahar. However, rumors do not come from nowhere, or perhaps some people do not want the Hebei-Chahar authorities to implement friendly relations with Japan, so they create all kinds of rumors in an attempt to undermine them. Rumors stop at the wise, and there is no need to defend them. Chairman Song's enthusiasm for the country is seen by all. I have a thorough understanding of the greatness of Chairman Song's personality. Chairman Song advocates that China and Japan should implement friendly relations, and I fully support lasting friendship. I would also like to do my best to facilitate and introduce them in order to promote them. Now, I would like to use the host's wine to wish Chairman Song good health, and to wish good health to everyone present." After Tashiro finished his reply, everyone applauded. Chinese and Western music was then played, including "Ten Thousand Years Song," "Drunken Peace," and "March," "Friendly Banquet," and "Happy Guests." The hosts and guests had a pleasant conversation and drink, and the gathering ended happily at 2:00 in the afternoon. (2nd)

Request for Re-examination of Bad Monk Rejected 67

Lianchi Temple on Wufeng Mountain in Mutu Township, Wuxian County, is one of the famous monasteries in Suzhou, with a flourishing incense offering. The abbot of the temple, Monk Kuanlu, privately built a secret room and engaged in improper behavior. The Wuxian Public Security Bureau verified this and ordered the expulsion of the bad monk, and the district office was ordered to select a replacement to take over. However, the monk resisted the transfer and refused to meet. On one hand, he pleaded with the monks of major temples to submit a petition to the county government to delay the sealing of the temple, but this was rejected. The township Baojia chief Ding Renlin and others believe that the township patrol officer is protecting the bad monk, so they submitted a petition to the county government on the 2nd to dismiss his followers. Kuanlu also submitted a petition to the county government, claiming that the Public Security Bureau's investigation was inaccurate and requesting that a qualified official be appointed to conduct a thorough re-examination to clarify the truth. The county government issued a reply on the 3rd, stating that the Public Security Bureau had already been ordered to carry out the expulsion and report it to the Second District Administrative Inspector's Office of Jiangsu Province, and that the Second District Office had been ordered to recruit a replacement. The request for re-examination should not be discussed.

Two Cases Filed and Handed Over to the County for Investigation 68

The First Branch of the Fifth Public Security Bureau discovered a den selling opium in Niuchangshang, Shanrenqiao Township, and confiscated eight packages of opium, smoking paraphernalia, and other items. Two opium traffickers, Cao Tuquan and his mother, Cao Chou, were arrested.
