Jiading: Car Overturns into River 69

At about 5:00 p.m. on the 1st, a Shanghainese man was driving his own sedan-style car back to Shanghai after traveling in Taicang. When passing by Huizhaqiao south of Malu Station in this county, the driver neglected his duty due to the windy and rainy weather and dark skies, and overturned into the river west of the road. The eight men and women in the car fell into the river with the car. The road workers repairing the road on the Xihu Road went to rescue them. Two of the children were already on the verge of death, but fortunately, there were no major injuries. After being rescued, they went to Nanxiang to change cars and return to Shanghai. The next day, a crane was dispatched from Shanghai to Jiading to salvage the car that had fallen into the river. However, due to the great weight, it could not be salvaged. To this day, the car is still in the river.

Memorial Monument Scheduled for Unveiling 70

Hou Tongzeng and Huang Tao'an, two martyrs of this county, advocated defending the city in righteousness during the late Ming Dynasty. They were unyielding during the Three Massacres and eventually died for their country. At a time when the country is in great difficulty, it is necessary to commend them. Therefore, educational staff and school students donated thousands of yuan to build the Hou Huang Two Loyal and Righteous Public Memorial Monument in Kuishan Park, which has now been completed. It is now scheduled to hold a grand unveiling ceremony on November 6th, the local memorial day. Wang Gongyu, the third administrative inspector commissioner, has been invited to Jiading to unveil the monument. A notice has been sent to all walks of life, and a grand occasion is expected at that time.

Changshu: The Bandit Gang of the Meili Robbery 71

Wang Xiangjiu and Gao Yunpan's family, wealthy households in Meili Tangqiao, were robbed by bandits a few weeks ago, suffering losses of three to four thousand gold. After the investigation team worked hard to investigate, Chen Youliang and Wang Agen were captured in the Shanghai Concession. They have now been brought to Changshu. The victims, Wang and Gao, went to the bureau to identify them and confirmed that they were the perpetrators. The clothes worn by the Wang bandit and the leather shoes worn by the Chen bandit were indeed the items lost by the family. With this ironclad evidence, the two bandits knew it was difficult to deny and immediately confessed that they had committed a total of nine robberies, including the houses of He Fu in Yaozhen, He Fengxi in Hejiashi, and He She in Taoshe. The gang confessed that they were lake bandits from the Xianzi Mountain gang in the Taihu Lake area of Suzhou, totaling four to five hundred people. The investigation team has confirmed the confession and is now coordinating with the authorities to apprehend the remaining bandits. The captured criminals will be handed over to the county judicial authorities for review.

Changzhou: Two Banks Exchange Copper Coins 72

The eight industries of Wujin County, including wine sauce and cigarettes, previously had an overabundance of copper coins in circulation, causing financial stagnation. They jointly sent the accumulated copper coins to the Changzhou branches of the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications for exchange. Subsequently, Chiang Wei-hsien, chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, agreed with the authorities of the two branches to exchange 10,000 yuan first within one week, and convened representatives of the eight industries on the 30th of last month to discuss the distribution plan and whether it was necessary to retain the balance to facilitate the exchange of other industries. It was decided that the Chamber of Commerce would first complete the exchange before discussing the distribution method. The County Chamber of Commerce then sent a letter to the two branches requesting them to send personnel to the meeting to collect the exchange. Yesterday (2nd), the two branches sent personnel to begin inspecting the exchange, but the procedures are extremely complicated and will take half a month to complete.

Wujiang: Major Fire in Tongli Town 73

Yesterday (1st) at 7:00 or 8:00 a.m., Yang Yuanchang's paper candle shop in Dongdai, Tongli Town, Wujiang County, caught fire carelessly, and the flames burst through the roof and could not be stopped. The fire spread to over thirty houses across the street, including Mabaohe Silver Shop, Jinlun Foreign Goods Store, Nantaitai Native Products Store in Nandai, Yuankang Clothing Store, Dechang Beijing Goods Store, and Fuan Tea House. Although the fire brigades from various sections tried their best to put out the fire, the streets were too narrow and the wind and fire were dry, making it difficult to extinguish. The shops in this section are the busiest in the town, with losses exceeding 200,000 yuan. The fire was not extinguished until 12:00 a.m. The public security branch is investigating the cause of the fire in order to determine responsibility.

Wuxi: Coordinating Rice Stem Borer Control Efforts 74

The Second District Administrative Commissioner's Office, in accordance with a resolution of the First Administrative Conference, ordered all counties to coordinate rice stem borer control efforts and reported to the provincial government for instructions and supervision. Now that the winter rice stem borer control work has begun, it is urgent to study the coordination methods of the counties in order to achieve the goal of eliminating pests. It is scheduled to hold a meeting on the 10th of this month to discuss this matter. A special order was issued yesterday to each county to appoint agricultural officials to attend and participate in the discussion, and to prepare coordination methods before the meeting for review and discussion at the meeting.

Eight-County Construction Conference 75

The Administrative Commissioner's Office, upon receiving instructions from the Executive Yuan through the Provincial Government, should devote itself to the central work of the construction undertaking from this year, with each period of three months. Each period must be carried out in accordance with the predetermined plan. The scope of the central work should be based on road construction, afforestation, land reclamation, water conservancy, disaster prevention, telephone, and electricity. Within the scope, the most important ones should be selected based on the local conditions, time, people, and events, and a plan should be formulated and submitted for approval. Zang Qifang, the commissioner, decided to convene a meeting on the morning of the 10th of this month, with the county magistrates, construction bureau chiefs, and construction personnel of the eight counties under its jurisdiction to discuss. Before the meeting, each county should prepare a plan based on the local situation, in accordance with the standard scope, and submit it for review.

Jiangyin: Trial Judge Shen Yuan Accused 76

Shen Qingchen from Gushan, Wudong, the current manager of the Licheng Steamboat Bureau, was arrested and detained by the county in the case of Song Qichen, the owner of Changjing, selling red pill drugs last year, and was sentenced to two years and six months imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 yuan by the Provincial Garrison Headquarters. He has served fourteen months. In August, the trial judge Shen Yuan suddenly granted bail, and someone accused Judge Shen of illegally releasing the key drug criminal, with suspicion of bribery. The High Court then ordered the Wuxi District Court to send Judge Lai Sihe to Cheng yesterday (2nd) to investigate the county government, and inquired in detail with the guarantor Cai Xuelin and the enforcement policeman Zhu Qixin. There were already clues about this case, and he returned to Wuxi in the afternoon to report.

The Xicheng long-distance bus, which departed from Wuxi to Cheng at about 12:00 a.m. on the 1st, had a Japanese man dressed in Chinese casual clothes. Yangzhou: Notice of Levy for Land Tax 80

The land tax for 1936 in Jiangdu was announced on the 1st. All land with inconsistent land tax has been reported to the provincial government, and approval is pending for correction in the next year. After this reorganization, the land tax seems to be improving.

Construction of Jingcheng Road 81

The Jiangdu County Construction Committee held its fourth committee meeting at the county government at 2:00 p.m. on the 2nd. Resolutions included: (1) The construction of Jingcheng Road, starting from Puqi Road, passing through Andun Lane, along the Lotus Pond, through the city wall, Daxibei Road, Xifu West Street, Shuangjing Lane, through the city wall, through Luyang Village to Fenghuangqiao Town, first opening the new north and south city gates, and building the Luyang Bridge. Regarding the demolition of houses, start from Nanmenwai and divide the passing places into several sections, and demolish them in stages. Residents whose houses are demolished should be compensated for their losses. The project cost of this road is set at 68,095.20 yuan. (2) The construction of Tianzhao Road, starting from Chao Guan to Tianningmen, to reach the scenic area, as the north-south trunk road of the new city. (3) The construction of Guanxi Road, as the main east-west road of the county, east across the canal to Aizijie, and connecting with Puqi Road, west out of the west gate to Tongyang Road, passing through Dongguan Street, Caiyi Street, Dadongmen Street, and Ximen Avenue. Regarding the demolition of houses, it will also be carried out in stages.

Zhenjiang: Tiger Sighted on Zhenju Road 82

The area from Zhenjiang to Jurong is undulating with mountains and continuous mountains. In previous years, it was known as the most desolate and dangerous area. Since the opening of Zhenju Road, it has become a major artery for traffic between Nanjing and Zhenjiang. The population has increased, and the number of travelers is dense. Tigers and leopards have disappeared, and bandits have disappeared. However, the area around Qiaojiamenxi Huifeng An Fenlonggang Lime Kiln is still steep and densely covered with weeds, and there are still wild beasts lurking. Recently, Secretary-General Luo of the Provincial Government saw a tiger with mottled patterns and a body like a calf when he passed the Fenlonggang Lime Kiln area by private car. When he saw the car, he fled into the mountains in surprise. Yesterday, Chen Zhongxi also saw this beast in the same place when he went to Nanjing via Jurong. If no measures are taken to hunt and kill it, it will seriously affect the safety of the villagers. Yesterday, Zhang, the magistrate of Zhenjiang, was specially instructed to instruct his subordinates and nearby hunters to find a way to capture it, so as to avoid harming people and livestock and ensure the safety of the villages.

Haizhou: Investigating Kala-azar in Haizhou 83

The Health Experimental Department of the National Economic Commission has recently dispatched Sun Zhicheng, the leader of the Kala-azar Research Team in Qingjiangpu, to Xuhai District and Lu Yu and other provinces to investigate the situation of Kala-azar, because Kala-azar is spreading widely. Sun has already departed from Qingjiang yesterday to Haizhou. His investigation focuses on: (1) The spread of Kala-azar; (2) The origin of Kala-azar; (3) Treatment methods for Kala-azar; (4) Whether Kala-azar in the East Sea area is the same as Kala-azar in the Huaiyin area; (5) Whether Kala-azar in the East Sea area is transmitted by sandflies; (6) The number of patients; (7) The number of deaths; (8) Research on the source and prevention and control methods of Kala-azar. After the East Sea area is investigated, he will go to Xuzhou, Lu, and Yu.

Jiaxing A Long Drought Hails Sweet Rain 84

Jiaxing had been without rain for a long time, the rivers dried up, and the fields cracked. Many crops in the countryside, such as beans and vegetables, withered. The late rice also couldn't mature fully due to lack of rain. Beans and wheat couldn't even be sown. Residents also lacked drinking water, making it difficult to fetch water. The air was dry, causing eye and throat ailments. People had been hoping for rain for a long time. It finally began to drizzle around 2 AM three days ago, and there was still a hint of rain at noon. The countryside rejoiced at this rain. From now on, beans, wheat, and other crops can be sown, and the spread of common ailments can also be slightly suppressed.

Hangzhou Rushing to Build Border Highways 85

The southeastern border of Zhejiang Province is adjacent to Fujian and Jiangxi provinces. Due to its location in high mountains and inconvenient transportation, bandit gangs often emerged. To facilitate the suppression of bandits, the Construction Department has strictly ordered the construction of various highways to be expedited. (1) The Lishui to Songyang section has been fully completed and opened to traffic, and commercial operations began at the end of October, with excellent results. (2) The original road surface of the Songyang to Suichang section has been completed and only needs to be tidied up and bridges built. It can be completed by the end of December. (3) Earthwork for the Yongjia, Ruian, and Pingyang road was once collected from civilian laborers, but work was suspended midway due to some reason. Now, it has been decided to continue construction and complete the entire project by the end of the year.

Zhejiang Rice Seizures Allowed for Release 86

The autumn harvest in Zhejiang Province this year has been abundant in various counties, and the output of agricultural products has increased. However, rice prices have risen daily, causing considerable panic among ordinary people. The authorities learned that a large quantity of rice was being shipped out of Jiaxing, Pinghu, Jiashan, and other rice-producing areas in Zhejiang, supposedly for export overseas. Therefore, they ordered the counties to seize all rice to maintain the food supply for the people. Now, after merchants appealed and it was verified that the rice was being transported to Shanghai for sale and certified by the Chamber of Commerce, the Civil Affairs Department has ordered the counties to allow the release for export to facilitate the circulation of food and regulate the market.

Ningbo Ban on Exporting Food Grains 87

The Zhenhai County government, considering that the county's food supply is insufficient and sometimes relies on imports from other counties for relief, has always strictly prohibited unauthorized exports. However, recently, some unscrupulous merchants, only concerned with profit and disregarding the people's food supply, have been secretly smuggling goods for export. Yesterday, special instructions were issued to the heads of each Public Security Bureau to supervise the police at stations and wharves to pay special attention. If anyone lacks a transportation permit issued by the government and promulgated by the province, regardless of whether they have declared and paid taxes, they will be immediately detained. At the same time, a letter was sent to the customs and various shipping companies to jointly prevent it.

Sports News

British World Games Football Report Claims: British New Tactics Not Superior, Strongly Advocates the Need to Re-Adopt Old Methods, Football Association Revises Referee Memorandum 88

Reuters, London -- A major surprise at the British Football Association Congress was the report on the British football team's disastrous defeat in Berlin. The report strongly stated that the British style of play is not superior to other countries. The "W" formation does not find favor in most European countries.

The report, signed by Wallraf White and Rose, clearly expresses the opinion of most British officials that the methods adopted by Austria, Norway, and Poland are more effective than those of Britain.

The report stated that, in general, the old method, with its emphasis on attack over defense, has proven to be more effective, and the game is certainly more interesting to watch. There is considerable reason to believe that British professional teams will revert to the football style they had for a long time in the past this season. The initial change was entirely to adapt to the changed offside rule. If this is indeed the case, the results of British international football matches will inevitably improve accordingly. This time, the discussions in Berlin between senior British football officials and the International Football Association on various issues arising in international football management are considered a serious matter. Therefore, it may allow the British Football Association to rejoin the International Football Association. Currently, the two sides have only established a "gentleman's agreement" on exchanging players. Another result of the British Football Association Congress was the publication of a revised memorandum regarding linesmen and referees, which contains clear instructions on how to work. The "diagonal" system favored by the Referees Committee allows referees to always know the position of their assistants. There should be extremely close cooperation among these three officials.

Instructions for Referees

The memorandum makes several important conclusions regarding the referee's management of players, with the following specific instructions:

(1) Referees can exercise their own discretion in dealing with rough actions and are authorized to stop them in various ways.

(2) When a player is cautioned, the player's name and the word "caution" must be used simultaneously, and the player must be made aware that this is their last chance.

(3) When warning or verbally cautioning a player, the referee should not point a finger or place their hand on any player.

(4) Referees must stop rough behavior at the outset.

(5) Referees must punish intentional acts, not unintentional ones.

(6) After issuing a ruling, the referee cannot change it. If there are any doubts, they should consult with the linesmen before issuing the ruling.

(7) Players must not obstruct the referee's decisions. Those who obstruct or express anger must be cautioned.

(8) Referees should not discuss or debate incidents with players or officials on the field, nor should they discuss or debate with any players off the field.

(9) Any penalty that favors the side committing a foul should not be implemented. The memorandum pays special attention to the game method of "wasting time," which is completely contrary to the spirit of the game and has become noteworthy.

When taking free kicks and throw-ins, players kick the ball wildly to allow their team to regain their position and monitor their opponents. The memorandum considers this habit childish and annoying and asks referees to firmly deal with such actions that violate the spirit of football.

Chinese Sports Federation Tennis Finals: Shanghai Jiang High School Retains Championship, 2-1 Result, Guanghua Second Place, Shanghai Jiang Wins Two Singles, Guanghua Wins Doubles 90

The seventh Municipal Middle School Sports Federation Tennis Championship, with the participation of four schools including Private Shanghai, Fushi, Guanghua, and Shanghai Jiang, began its preliminary round the day before yesterday. Private Shanghai and Fushi were both eliminated. Shanghai Jiang and Guanghua, who qualified for the finals, were delayed by rain the day before yesterday and only held the finals at the Municipal Sports Field at 2:00 PM yesterday. As a result, Shanghai Jiang won two singles matches, and Guanghua won the doubles match. The overall result was 2-1, and Shanghai Jiang won the championship. According to previous reports, the champion was Guanghua High School, and the previous champion was Shanghai Jiang. In total, Shanghai Jiang has retained two championship titles. The battle results are as follows:

Tang Baojia Defeats Xiong Dazuan First Single: Shanghai Jiang's Tang Baojia vs. Guanghua's Xiong Dazuan. Tang was injured playing basketball the night before and could barely take a step yesterday. His ball skills were not as sluggish as in the hard-court cycle week the day before. Xiong is one of Guanghua's fierce generals and was quite unwilling to submit. In the first set, he resisted Tang in every way. Tang narrowly took advantage of him midway, handled it carefully afterward, and finally defeated Xiong 6-3 in the first set. Tang's spirit was even stronger in the second set, invincible, and won another slippery set, thus winning 2-0.

Chen Dexian Defeats Wang Tianduo Shanghai Jiang's Chen met Guanghua's Wang in the second single. The strength of both sides was equal, and there were many wonderful and tense moments. The first set was even more difficult to separate, with frequent ties. Chen, with his accurate landing points, won three consecutive games and ended the set 7-5. In the second set, Wang's spirit was greatly reduced. After winning two games, he immediately collapsed and lost again 6-2. The overall result was 2-0, and the championship was lost from then on.

Guanghua Wins One Doubles Match The final doubles match was irrelevant to the overall result. Shanghai Jiang sent Xu Peizhi and Zhang Dechang, who had defeated Fushi with two 6-3 scores the day before. Their ball skills were experienced, and they immediately gave Guanghua's Feng Zhuomin and Sun Luofang a blow with a 6-1 score. However, Feng and Sun were not discouraged by this, calmly responded, and finally tied the score 6-1, making the autumn colors evenly divided. The final deciding set was even more exciting. From 4-4 to 5-5, and then 6-6, Feng and Sun cooperated effectively and finally completed two games in one go, achieving success with a score of 8-6. The overall result was 2-1, Guanghua winning the doubles.

Most Popular Public Reading Material: Shanghai Comic Book Industry, Over a Thousand Products, Mostly Focused on Gods and Monsters, Ministry of Education is Planning to Improve and Promote Social Education 100

Comic books are the most popular reading material among the public, especially those published in Shanghai. However, most of the content is supernatural novels, which has a significant impact on the promotion of social education. The Ministry of Education is now working to improve this. Details are as follows:

Publication Types The content of comic books is mostly based on old novels, simplifying them, popularizing them, and making them interesting, with half the content being text and half being illustrations. Occasionally, news events that occur in society are compiled into comics. Most of the content is supernatural and legendary, such as "Seven Swords and Thirteen Heroes," "Wild River Heroine," and "Burning the Red Lotus Temple." There are many titles, but obscene works are relatively rare. Since the target audience is children and adults with rudimentary literacy, chivalrous novels are more attractive.

Industry Overview There are no less than a hundred bookstores in the city that publish comic books, and most of them are located in the Beigongyi Lane of Mongolia Road in Zhabei. There are as many as eighty or ninety stores there. There are also several stores in Nine Acres. Only one store is on Dalu Road. The total number of published types is eight or nine hundred, each ranging from one to more than ten volumes. Wholesale sales to other cities are very prosperous, especially to the north. Those who sell in the city are all book vendors in various neighborhoods, used to roughly provide nearby residents with reading material. The lowest price averages from seven cents to one jiao per volume.

Significant Impact Although comic books are not noticed by the general intellectual class, they have a great influence among the lower class and children. Because they are popular, simple, and interesting, they are almost everywhere. Students in shops and factories are particularly fond of renting these readings. However, because of the supernatural and legendary content, children's thinking is changed by it, which is no less effective than supernatural films. It is indeed the most popular reading material among the public.

Finding Ways to Improve Educational circles consider comic books to be a useful tool for promoting social education. Therefore, there have been several attempts to improve them in recent years, such as the Shanghai Social Education Society and the Children's Bookstore, which have published improved comic books. It is recently heard that the Ministry of Education is also paying close attention to this and is planning to revise them.

Tao Baichuan's Speech: How to Revive Chinese Culture - At the Sino-Foreign Cultural Association 104

The Sino-Foreign Cultural Association recently held a social gathering, and specially invited Mr. Tao Baichuan, who had just returned from a study tour in Europe and America, to give a speech on "How to Revive Chinese Culture." A record of his speech is as follows:

Study of Foreign Cultures Reveals Two Points Worth Noting

Before the establishment of the Sino-Foreign Cultural Association, I had already participated in the Cultural Construction Association. At that time, ten professors advocated native culture. What exactly is China's native culture? Although its essence and definition were not clearly defined, it aroused considerable attention in all circles for a time. Later, I went abroad to study foreign cultures and found two points worth noting: (1) Pay attention to the people's lives; (2) Establish a solid economic foundation. All countries pay close attention to the people's lives, especially in the Soviet Union, where this is particularly evident. They pay special attention to the lives of children, women, and the working masses. Nurseries and kindergartens can be seen everywhere. The national character of the German people tends towards militarism and iron-bloodedness. Only with such a nation can there be such a Germany. Therefore, how should we start to promote the revival of Chinese culture? I believe that in addition to politics and economics, we must explore and seek conclusions in the area of people's lives. Because politics, economics, and the people's basic needs of food, clothing, shelter, and transportation are all elements that constitute culture. Are the physique and spirit of the Chinese people adapted to the modern world? Under the impact of the two forces of the left and right, can our nation stand its ground? Can we save the country from the brink of collapse? Can the whole country still strive to improve our lives?

To Promote Culture, One Must First Study People's Lives

The object of the people's lives should be all systems, cultural relics, institutions, and customs. Culture can certainly influence people's lives, but ultimately culture is created by people. Therefore, to promote culture, one must first study people's lives. My feeling after studying various countries is that we should: (1) Promote the people's health. We cannot discover our own shortcomings without comparing ourselves with others. The results of this World Games and the struggles that occurred show that the Chinese people cannot survive unless they start with health. Taking football as an example, the failure of our players is due to their lack of physical endurance. Therefore, we must strive for physical health in life, in addition to politics and economics, in order to find a way out. If the Chinese people do not improve their health, they will perish without being invaded by others. (2) Cultivate the people's spirit of struggle. In the World Games, our football team failed due to lack of physical strength, while our basketball team failed due to lack of unwavering fighting spirit. When the draw resulted in playing Japan first, the players' spirits were immediately dampened, and the result was failure. Our basketball team had previously performed very well in competitions with American basketball teams. This time, psychological failure led to factual failure. After returning to China, I had the same feeling when I saw the diplomatic situation. I have talked with Shen Junru, Li Gongpu, and others in the National Salvation Association. They believe that the purpose of the National Salvation Association is to promote resistance against Japan, but there is still a problem that the government is not ready yet, so it cannot promote resistance against Japan. But we must cultivate the spirit of resistance against Japan. The reason why the Jewish people cannot restore their country is that the nation lacks the spirit of struggle. German youths all wear uniforms, and everyone carries a knife and hangs portraits of famous people, both literary and military, everywhere. They also wear swords. The Soviet Union also pays great attention to cultivating the spirit of struggle in children's training. Everything is man-made. The country is built by people. Therefore, the culture of a country is the life of the people.

To Promote a Country's Culture, Attention Should Be Paid to the Economy

The first point we should pay attention to is the economy, which is the foundation of everything. Politics and education are the upper levels, while the economy is the lower foundation. To change or promote a country's culture, one must rely on the economy. The Soviet Union is indeed a new society. Regardless of whether you oppose it or support it, you cannot deny that they have new constructions. They have kitchen factories specializing in cooking. They want women to run from the kitchen to the factory. Farms must first relieve them of their kitchen work at home. After women finish their work, they can go to the kitchen factory to buy cooked food. Soviet families now have no kitchens. Women have four months of leave during childbirth, and light industry also has three days of leave. When a child is two months old, he or she can be sent to a nursery. Nurseries accept children of several levels: two months old or older, five months old or older, one year old or older, and two years old or older. At the age of three, they go to kindergarten. Women are liberated from the family, so they can contribute their labor to society. If China wants to revive the nation and promote culture, it cannot achieve its goal without improving the people's lives and the national economy. As the people's lives are gradually improved and the national economy is gradually built, culture will be within it. We do not have to learn from other countries' left-leaning tendencies, nor do we have to imitate other countries' right-leaning tendencies. Although the Kuomintang has periods of military administration and tutelage, it must move towards constitutionalism.

Shanghai Municipal Council Primary School Overview (III) Special Report by This Newspaper: Hu Zuyin's Investigation 105

The service regulations for faculty and staff of each school, as well as the detailed rules for the service of principals, academic directors, teachers, and clerks, have been stipulated and will not be repeated here. The daily work of faculty and staff at school has also been specified in detail. The work is divided into three categories: work at the beginning of the semester, work after the start of school, and work after school. The work after the start of school is further divided into four types: daily work, weekly work, monthly work, and every six weeks of work. All faculty and staff of each school are full-time employees and may not hold any paid positions outside the school. Faculty and staff must abide by the service creed and all regular rules.

In addition to performing their own teaching duties, faculty and staff must participate in various relevant meetings in the school. The school's meetings include the school affairs meeting and the teaching affairs meeting, which discuss all issues related to school affairs and teaching affairs. There are also high-grade, middle-grade, low-grade, and kindergarten education research meetings to discuss teaching matters related to each grade. There are also guidance committees, admissions committees, graduate guidance committees, and Boy Scout affairs committees, etc., to discuss and handle matters within the scope of each committee.

5. Qualifications and Treatment of Faculty and Staff

According to the Shanghai Municipal Council Primary School Faculty and Staff Employment and Treatment Regulations, principals must have a degree from a domestic or foreign university's education department, education college, education department, or normal university, and have served in the education field for more than three years, and have considerable writings or achievements. The qualifications of the academic director are the same as those of the principal, and they enjoy the treatment of first-class teachers. Second-class teachers must have a degree from a domestic university and be engaged in full-time teaching. Third-class teachers must be graduates of normal colleges and secondary normal schools or secondary specialized schools and be engaged in specialized teaching. Clerks are divided into two grades: second grade and third grade. They must be graduates of secondary schools or have equivalent academic qualifications, be able to calculate school accounts, and be able to handle Chinese and English documents. The number of faculty and staff in Shanghai Municipal Council Primary School is now copied and recorded according to grade as follows:

Shanghai Municipal Council Primary School Faculty and Staff Number Survey Table (Surveyed in July 1936)

In terms of treatment, the salary of formally employed faculty and staff is based on individual qualifications and the position held, as specified below:

Shanghai Municipal Council Primary School Faculty and Staff Salary Standard Table (in yuan)

Faculty and staff are responsible for their own board and lodging. However, if there are suitable houses in the school and they voluntarily live in them, the accommodation fee may be deducted from their monthly salary according to the following standards.

Other benefits include seniority bonuses, vacation salaries, medical subsidies, and retirement savings. Faculty and staff who have been employed for more than one year will receive an additional half-month's salary as a seniority bonus every New Year's Day; however, the seniority bonus for those with a monthly salary of more than 200 yuan is limited to 100 yuan. In addition, faculty and staff who have been employed for more than one year and resign with the approval of the Municipal Council may receive one month's vacation salary; those who resign before being employed for one year will have their salary calculated up to the date of termination of their position or teaching duties. Faculty and staff who are hospitalized for illness in the Municipal Council Hospital or a hospital designated by the Municipal Council will be subsidized by the Municipal Council for medical expenses of $1.25 per day. Female staff members or female teachers who are pregnant and give birth may apply for a long leave of one semester (seven months). No salary will be paid during the leave. After returning to work after the leave, in addition to not counting the leave period, their length of service will still be calculated as continuous employment.

Retirement savings are made by each school's faculty and staff by deducting 5% of their monthly salary, which is stored by the Municipal Council as retirement savings. The Municipal Council adds twice the amount of the retirement savings deducted by each employee each month, merges and stores them, and also provides a fixed annual interest rate of 6% on the savings. Depositors who meet one of the following conditions may recover all of the retirement savings and interest paid by the Municipal Council; otherwise, depositors may only recover their own retirement savings and interest:

1. Those who have joined the savings plan for more than three years and apply for resignation with the approval of the Municipal Council.

2. Those who are disabled due to illness or injury in the line of duty, and are certified by the Municipal Council's doctor as unable to continue working.

3. Those who have been continuously employed for 20 years and apply for resignation with the approval of the Municipal Council.

In addition to the above benefits, there are also funeral expenses, death benefits, disability benefits, and retirement pensions. If a faculty or staff member of each school dies in the line of duty, their successor or legal representative may receive funeral expenses of 60 yuan from the Municipal Council; they may also receive from the Municipal Council an amount equal to 5% of the employee's annual salary at the time of death multiplied by the number of years of service as death benefits. If they are disabled due to illness in the line of duty, and are certified by the Municipal Council's doctor as unable to continue working, and are guaranteed by the head of the department as having always been cautious in their work, they may receive from the Municipal Council an amount equal to 5% of the annual salary at the time of retirement multiplied by the number of years of service as disability benefits. Those who have been employed for 20 years and have been approved to resign by the Municipal Council may receive from the Municipal Council an amount equal to 5% of the annual salary at the time of retirement multiplied by the number of years of service as retirement pensions.

6. Teacher Training Methods

In addition to teaching, teachers at Municipal Council Primary Schools must participate in various training activities. Each school has a teacher library, and various books, newspapers, and magazines that teachers should read are added every year. The Chinese Education Department compiles and prints an index of educational books and papers every month and distributes it to teachers in each school for reference. After reading the books, teachers must also make a written report and submit it to the Chinese Education Department for review. During the winter and summer vacations, teachers in each school have assigned vacation work, such as collecting teaching materials for each subject, compiling teaching units, and reading various books and newspapers.

Every Saturday afternoon, teachers of each subject in each school jointly hold subject-based research meetings to participate in research together. Several lectures are held during each semester, and celebrities are hired by the Chinese Education Department to give lectures, and teachers from each school must attend. Each school also has off-campus visits, and teachers take turns to participate, visiting famous schools in and outside the city, large-scale organizations and factories, and various exhibitions. After the teachers visit, they make written reports separately, compile teaching materials, or collect teaching aids as a reference for improving teaching.

Teachers in each school also pay attention to their own health. After school every afternoon, male and female teachers often participate in various extracurricular activities in groups. Each school currently has teacher tennis teams, basketball teams, football teams, table tennis teams, volleyball teams, and quoits teams. The Chinese Education Department often holds various teacher sports competitions during each semester, in which teachers from each school participate separately, competing fairly and winning, in order to improve health and promote emotional connections.

Correction: In the Shanghai Municipal Council Primary School Overview (II) published yesterday, paragraph four should be paragraph two, and paragraph two should be the last paragraph of the article. Also, "School Buildings and Equipment" should be changed to Section 3.

Chairman Lin Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday to Pay Condolences for Mr. Duan Qirui's Death. He Also Asked Lu Zhong'an to Examine His Body 109

Chairman Lin Sen of the National Government left Nanjing on the night train at 11:00 PM the night before, attached to a flower car, and arrived in Shanghai at 6:50 AM yesterday. Yang Hu, Commander of the Songhu Garrison; Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government; Ji Zhangjian, Commander of the Security Corps; Cai Jingjun, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau; and Wang Zhinan, Secretary of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, and many others went to the Zhenru train station to welcome him. The Municipal Public Security Bureau specially sent a military band to the station to play music to welcome him. The Security Corps dispatched a company to Zhenru Railway Station and along Jiaotong Road to set up posts and strictly guard the area.

Condolences for Mr. Duan

After Chairman Lin got off the train, he was accompanied by Yang Hu, Commander of the Songhu Garrison, to Duan Qirui's residence on Avenue Joffre to pay his condolences. He then returned to his private residence on Jin Shenfu Road to rest. Yang accompanied him back to his residence and left after a brief conversation.

Examination of the Body

Chairman Lin then went to the Sino-Western Sanitarium on Rue Pu Shi at 9:40 AM to have his body examined. He was personally examined by the national physician Lu Zhong'an. It was not until 11:10 AM that the examination was completed, and he returned to his residence for lunch. According to Lu Zhong'an, Chairman Lin's health is good, and he only felt slightly tired. He has already prepared a conditioning formula to help him recover.

Visiting Friends

After returning to his residence for lunch at noon, Chairman Lin took the medicine prescribed by Lu Zhong'an and took a nap. In the afternoon, he got up and went out to visit friends until about 5:30 PM, when he returned to his residence to rest.

Chairman's Remarks

A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Chairman Lin yesterday evening and was received by him. Although the Chairman is old, he is still in good spirits. According to Chairman Lin, he has been away from Shanghai for ten months, and he has been taking the medicine prescribed by Dr. Lu Zhong'an for ten months. Recently, as the weather has gradually turned cold, the elderly inevitably feel some changes, so he made a special trip to Shanghai to have Dr. Lu Zhong'an examine his body and prescribe a new formula for him to continue taking. After taking the medicine just now, he felt quite comfortable. The reporter then asked him about his views on the overall situation. The Chairman did not want to express much on this, but said that protecting the family can protect the country, and protecting the country can protect the family. The two are inseparable. The traditional concept of the Chinese people is to value the family and despise the country, but they do not know that without a country, how can there be a family? This traditional concept is actually wrong, but this traditional concept has changed in recent years. During President Chiang's birthday, the people of the whole country enthusiastically contributed to the purchase of airplanes to dedicate to the country, which is enough to prove. He (Chairman Lin) is deeply gratified by this.

Opportunities for Chinese Goods in the Nanyang Market. Dutch Reduce Tariffs, Dutch Ships Appropriately Reduce Freight Rates 114

Java, Surabaya, Semarang, and other ports in the Dutch East Indies have always been major producers of sugar, and the daily necessities of their native people must be supplied by other countries. Chinese goods such as cement and wheat flour are shipped to Java in large quantities. However, in the gradual promotion of this business, the value of the Dutch currency suddenly fell, causing a major blow to Chinese goods arriving in Nanyang. The value of one Chinese dollar has always been 43 Dutch cents, but now it can be exchanged for 54 Dutch cents. As a result, the selling price of Chinese goods shipped to Nanyang has invisibly increased by 25%. This not only affects the livelihood of the local natives, but also hinders Chinese commercial goods. The Dutch government has organized a special committee to discuss how to remedy the lives of the people, suppress prices, and prevent the decline in currency value from hindering the import of daily necessities. After deliberation, it was decided to reduce import tariffs, and it was resolved to implement this from the 1st of this month. The tax reduction methods are divided into two categories: one is to shorten the import surtax, and the other is to reduce the import tax. Generally, it is reduced by about 20%. For goods assessed for import, the surtax was originally 50%, but it has now been changed to 25%. Cotton yarn with no printing of 45 pieces will also be specially reduced by 20%. As for the import tax, it must be reduced by about half. For example, the import of flour, which was originally taxed at 12%, is now taxed at only 6%. Shirts, etc., which were originally taxed at 12%, are now changed to 6%. Foreign yarn, which was originally taxed at 10%, is now reduced to 6%. Shanghai homespun cloth, which was originally taxed at 12%, is now also changed to 6%. Blankets, etc., are also changed to 6%. The import tariff is reduced to suppress the selling price, so that Chinese goods shipped to Nanyang can pay less import tax and not be affected by the decline in the guilder price. This new tariff has been sent to Shanghai to notify all industries. It has been found that the Nanyang liners of Chinese shipping companies should also announce a reduction in prices at the same time. The first class fare from Shanghai to Hong Kong is 100 yuan, the second class fare is reduced from 50 yuan to 45 yuan, the third class fare is reduced from 30 yuan to 27.5 yuan, and the steerage fare is reduced from 17.5 yuan to 15 yuan. The first class fare to Xiamen is 75 yuan, the second class fare is reduced from 50 yuan to 45 yuan, the third class fare is reduced from 30 yuan to 27 yuan, and the steerage fare is 12.5 yuan.

Ministry of Industry Promotes Fishery Bank Group. Qian Xinzhi and Others Go to Beijing for Consultations. Three Banks Continue to Lend 120,000 Yuan. 115

In order to relieve the fishing industry, the Ministry of Industry has specially joined forces with the Shanghai financial community to establish a Fishery Bank Group. All organizational regulations, etc., have been approved by the Executive Yuan. However, due to preparations for the Rural Bank, the establishment was delayed. However, in response to the needs of fishermen, the China, New China, and Four Lines Savings Banks have each allocated 40,000 yuan in funds, totaling 120,000 yuan, to lend to fishermen. It is learned that the Ministry of Industry believes that the bank group is one of the most effective ways to relieve the fishing industry and should not be delayed any further. Therefore, it specially sent letters to Qian Xinzhi of the Shanghai Four Lines Savings Bank, Qian Yanfang of the China Bank, Wang Zhihua of the New China Bank, etc., urging them to contact various participating banks and raise and pay the funds pledged, totaling 250,000 yuan, as soon as possible, so that the bank group can be established as soon as possible. Qian Xinzhi, Wang Zhihua, Xu Xinliu, and others went to Beijing the day before yesterday to attend the second board meeting of the Rural Bank, and will take the opportunity to discuss the implementation methods with Wu Dingchang, Minister of Industry. After returning to Shanghai, they will convene a meeting of representatives of various participating banks, and then formally establish the bank group on a scheduled date. Before the formal establishment of the Fishery Bank Group, the 120,000 yuan of fishery loans from the China, New China, and Four Lines Savings Banks will continue to be lent. Since the start of lending, more than 50,000 yuan has been lent, mostly to the Ningbo Fishery Loan Cooperative. The loan procedures require the fisherman to apply to the three banks through the fish market wholesaler, and the fish market will provide a guarantee. After passing the review, the loan can be borrowed, with a maximum term of ten months and an interest rate of 9%, but it can be repaid in installments.

Zhejiang Province's Intentions in Banning Rice Explained in Reply to Local Association's Telegram 117

The Shanghai Local Association telegraphed the authorities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces on the 31st of last month, requesting the revocation of the clear order banning rice from leaving the province. It is now learned that Zhejiang Province has replied by telegram, stating: (Excerpt) "Your telegram is acknowledged. This province's restriction on rice leaving the province is purely to prevent smuggling to the sea and is by no means intended to impede domestic circulation. After disembarking, Ambassador Trautmann went directly to the German Legation on Huangpu Road to rest. In the evening, he attended a banquet hosted by German Consul General Kriebel and then, together with his wife and Embassy Secretary Mohr who had come from Nanjing, departed for Nanjing on the 11:00 PM night express train to meet Foreign Minister Zhang and report on his return to his post. Because the German Embassy had already moved from Beiping to Nanjing, he would remain stationed in Nanjing from then on and would not need to go to Beiping.

Talks During Stopover in Shanghai

Ambassador Trautmann met with a Xin Sheng News Agency reporter on the ship yesterday and made the following remarks: Ambassador Trautmann first stated that he had returned to Germany for a six-month leave, during which he met with German officials in Berlin and Hamburg, as well as individuals enthusiastic about Sino-German culture in the Far East Association. He noted that the German people were extremely excited about the participation of the Chinese delegation in the World Games held in Germany, but he expressed regret for any shortcomings in their hospitality. He mentioned that the art pieces he had collected and brought back from China were displayed and exhibited, and were warmly received by the German people, who praised them highly. He also pointed out that there were many Chinese students in Germany, which was a testament to the cultural ties between the two countries, and that Sino-German cultural relations had seen progress in recent years, which he would continue to strive for. He expressed his joy at being able to return to learn more about Chinese culture.

German-Russian Relations

The reporter then inquired about the German-Russian issue, noting that the two countries had been attacking each other, and the situation seemed very tense. Ambassador Trautmann stated that the various rumors about Germany and Russia were not to be believed. However, he said that Germany was an enemy of communism, opposed communism, and opposed Bolshevism, and that there were no other political issues between Germany and Russia.

German-Japanese Relations

He continued, stating that he had transited Japan during his trip but did not stop there, instead proceeding directly to China on the same ship, and therefore had not met with any Japanese officials. At this point, the reporter inquired about the relationship between Germany and Japan. Ambassador Trautmann stated that Germany wished to be friendly with Japan, just as it did with China, but that, standing in the position of Ambassador to China, he hoped for a particularly friendly relationship between China and Germany. Ambassador Trautmann also denied previous reports of a German-Japanese military alliance, stating that he had heard nothing of it.

Sino-Japanese Disputes

Ambassador Trautmann continued to answer questions from the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter, stating that he had only seen reports in the newspapers regarding the situation between China and Japan, and that negotiations were currently underway in Nanjing. He said that he had been away from his post for a long time and was not familiar with the current situation, so he was not in a position to comment. However, he said that he hoped that China and Japan could reach a mutual understanding and peacefully resolve everything.

Non-Recognition of Manchukuo

It was reported earlier that the Havas News Agency had reported that Germany was disappointed with the soybean agreement previously signed with the puppet "Manchukuo" because imports from Manchukuo to Germany had increased sharply while German exports to the puppet state had decreased. The reporter specifically raised this question with Ambassador Trautmann. Ambassador Trautmann declined to comment on this, but later stated that Germany would never recognize the puppet "Manchukuo," and that Germany's attitude remained the same and would not change. The Xin Sheng News Agency reporter finally inquired about Germany's return to the League of Nations. Ambassador Trautmann smiled and did not answer, and the interview concluded happily.

Duan Qirui's Funeral Tomorrow, Chairman Lin and Mayor Wu Visited Yesterday, Duan Residence Released Duan's Will Last Night 119

Following the death of Duan Qirui, former head of the Beijing government, the Duan residence's funeral arrangement committee was established yesterday, and Duan's will was released last night. Chairman Lin, Mayor Wu, and others visited to pay their respects yesterday, and over a hundred telegrams of condolence have been received from various locations outside the city. The details are as follows:

Chairman Lin and Others Personally Pay Condolences

Those who visited to pay their respects yesterday morning and afternoon included Chairman Lin of the National Government, Mayor Wu of this city, Police Chief Cai Jinjun, Yu Qiaqing, Gong Xinzhan, Huang Fu (represented by Xu Xiuzhi), Central Committee member Chu Minyi, Foreign Minister Zhang Qun's representative, Director Zhou Jue of the Shanghai Office, Feng Gengguang, Songhu Garrison Commander Yang Hu, Liu Chaowang, Han Yunbo, Li Guojie, Gong Zhenpeng, Zhu Hongzhi, Zhao Hengti, Xu Xiuzhi, Chief Judge Lu Yimei of the Local Court, Qian Xinzhi, Qu Wenliu, National Government Relief Committee Chairman Zhu Qinglan, Japanese national Funatsu, and over two hundred of Duan's former colleagues and friends.

Solemn and Respectful Funeral Hall Arrangement

The funeral hall was set up in the main hall of the residence. The remains were covered with silk curtains, and an altar with fruit, vegetable offerings, incense, and candles was placed in front. Below, various wreaths were arranged, including dozens from Chairman Lin, Mayor Wu, Commander Yang, Finance Minister Kong, Foreign Minister Zhang, Governor Zhang Jia'ao of the Bank of China, and Financial Decision-maker Xu Kan. Because Duan was a devout Buddhist in life, the funeral hall arrangement followed Buddhist rituals, which was quite solemn and respectful. In front of the hall, there was a Buddhist monk, and in a separate room, there were many Buddhist followers chanting scriptures. Visitors were led in by ushers and performed the customary rites.

Funeral Arrangement Committee Established Yesterday

The Duan residence, led by Duan's former colleagues Li Sihao, Wu Guangxin, Zeng Yunpei, Liang Zhongyi, Qu Wenliu, and over thirty others, organized the funeral arrangement committee at the Duan residence on Avenue Joffre. It was established yesterday and divided into three groups: document, administration, and reception, to manage all affairs.

Funeral Announcement Issued, Burial Tomorrow

Duan's remains are scheduled to be buried tomorrow at 2:00 PM. The funeral arrangement committee has issued the following funeral announcement: "The former Head of the Republic of China, Duan, passed away on November 2nd at 7-9 PM. The burial is scheduled for 2:00 PM on the 5th at this residence. Duan Residence Funeral Arrangement Committee, 1487 Avenue Joffre."

Eight Admonitions in the Will Regarding National Affairs

The original text of Duan's will is as follows: "Will of the Old Man Zhengdao. I am over seventy years old. In the event of my sudden demise, considering the principle of life's journey and death's return, I have no lingering concerns. However, looking around, the country is vast, the people are poor, and resources are exhausted, which is truly heartbreaking. I have never liked to talk much. In the past, the country may not fully remember my advice on moving firewood and preventing chimney fires. Now, based on the experience of a seasoned traveler, I offer a final warning, hoping that the people of the country will listen quietly and act diligently. Then, even if I die, I will live on, and my eyes will be closed in peace. Although the country is weak, there is hope for revival. The way to revival is also very simple: Do not lightly initiate political disputes based on personal opinions, do not engage in empty talk without considering practice, do not undertake unnecessary tasks and waste public funds, do not believe in extreme theories and shake the foundation of the country. Those who discuss diplomacy should not forget to strengthen national defense. Those who manage education should not forget to preserve the national essence. Those who manage families should not abandon the inherent etiquette. Those who seek knowledge should not be distracted by the superficial brilliance of fashion. Adhering to these eight admonitions will cope with all situations. The so-called self-reliance lies in this, and turning weakness into strength also lies in this. I have never engaged in production in my life. My descendants should understand my intention of enjoying the Tao and being content with poverty. Funerals should be thrifty. Dress me in a Buddhist robe and do not offer meat or fish as sacrifices. This will was written on the fifth day after the Mid-Autumn Festival of the Bingzi year at Zhengdao Residence on Avenue Joffre."

Jianghai Ship Frequently Encounters Danger Japanese Warship Creates Huge Waves, Runs Aground Waiting for High Tide to Escape 121

Ningjing: The Ningjing ship of Ning Shao Company of this port, with a deadweight of 1,693 tons and a draft of 16 feet 7.5 inches, is now loaded with salt and coal. Yesterday, the company received a telegram from the owner of Ningjing, stating that when the ship was docked at the Fuzhong Coal Pier to load and unload cargo, a Japanese warship passed by at full speed, using its 33-knot horsepower, causing extremely large autumn-wave-like waves on the calm river surface, causing the Ningjing to collide with the pier. The mooring bolt on the stern right side was broken, and the mooring wire even broke a section of the iron railing several feet long. The hull was damaged, and the pier was also damaged.

Lishun: The Lishun ship of Lishun Shipping Company is currently operating in the North China area. Yesterday, the company received a telegram from the owner, stating that Lishun ran aground twice consecutively in the harbor when leaving Yingkou Port for Dalian this time. The hull and wheel blades may have been damaged, but this can only be determined after personnel are sent for inspection.

Chunhe: The Chunhe ship, owned by He Fengxin Shipping Company, managed by Continental Industrial Company, has a deadweight of 1,765 tons and a draft of 17 feet 4 inches. It is currently loading salt in Haizhou. A telegram was received yesterday, stating that Chunhe ran aground at Chenjiagang on the evening of the 2nd when it set sail from Haizhou after loading all the salt. It is now waiting for high tide to try to get off the shoal.

Two Major Inventions on Spinning Machines, Lei Binglin Successfully Researches 122

Engineer Lei Binglin of Wing On Spinning Mill has been researching for many years and has recently made two major inventions on spinning machines: one is a double trumpet on the roving frame, and the other is a large drafting on the spinning frame. These two inventions have been practically tested at the Ansha factory, and the results are very good. Yesterday, the Cotton Textile Dyeing Experiment Hall of the Academia Sinica specially sent four textile experts, Chuandao Shen, Ren Shangwu, Li Zhuangshou, and Nie Guangyu, to visit. They said that these inventions could not only improve product quality and increase production but also reduce manufacturing costs, which is truly good news for the future of Chinese textiles. However, they were unwilling to disclose the detailed content because the inventions had just been submitted to the Ministry of Industry for patent application and had not yet been approved. According to reports, Lei studied textile engineering in the United States and served as a professor of textile engineering at Nantong University for 15 years and as an engineer at Wing On Spinning Mill for more than 10 years. He is currently about 60 years old, with a full head of white hair, but he is in very good spirits.

French Concession, Household Survey Procedures 125

The French Concession authorities have decided to start a sectional household survey within the concession by the police department starting from the 3rd of this month. This survey will start in the eastern district. Chinese household survey forms will be sent to each Chinese household on a scheduled basis and collected the next day. If the next day is a holiday, they will be collected the day after. After the subletters receive the form, they should fill in (1) the names of all persons staying overnight in the house on that day and (2) the names of those who regularly live in their home but work night shifts outside, and return the form. It is hoped that residents within the concession will strongly support the personnel responsible for the survey to facilitate its progress.

Guangdong Tobacco Industry Representatives Arrive in Shanghai, Soon to Petition in Nanjing, Petition in Nanjing to Abolish the Local Tobacco 126

Since the era of Chen Jitang's governance in Guangdong Province, most industries and businesses have been subject to unified control and monopoly for the purpose of collecting money. The tobacco monopoly is recognized as harmful to merchants and detrimental to farmers. After the unification of Guangdong and Guangxi, the Guangdong Tobacco Leaf and Tobacco Thread Associations and farmers from various regions have called for the abolition of the tobacco monopoly. However, the government has not adopted their requests. The tobacco merchants and farmers are greatly disappointed. They have held separate meetings to decide to send representatives to Nanjing to petition for the abolition of the tobacco monopoly. Representatives from the Tobacco Thread Association, Fang Yuwan, the Tobacco Leaf Association, Wu Yuqiang, Su Dingchuan, and the Heshan farmers representatives, Lu Yining, Chen Yiguang, and five others, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday aboard the Coolidge. In addition to appealing to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Guangdong Compatriots Association, and related organizations in this city for assistance, urging the government to abolish this harsh policy, they also plan to host the local press to explain the harms of the monopoly, with the aim of gaining unanimous support from the public opinion.

China National Aviation Corporation Ready, Shanghai-Hong Kong Flight to Start Tomorrow, One-Way Ticket 200 Yuan, Round-Trip 360 Yuan, Three Flights Per Week, Sino-British Simultaneous Flight, Ticket Sales Have Started, Passenger Booking is Enthusiastic 127

The China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) has established a station in Hong Kong and is about to start flying. After both China and the UK have negotiated properly, and the UK government issued a license, the company actively prepared. General Manager Dai Enji flew to Hong Kong some days ago to arrange everything and has returned to Shanghai. According to him, the establishment of CNAC station in Hong Kong has been arranged, and a Hong Kong office has been formally established to handle all matters regarding passenger and mail transportation between Shanghai and Hong Kong. The Shanghai-Hong Kong flight is scheduled to officially start on the 5th. It is said that ticket sales have started, and passenger seat reservations are very enthusiastic.

Flight Schedule and Ticket Prices

After establishing the Hong Kong station, the Shanghai-Guangdong-Hong Kong flight schedule has been revised as follows: A. (Southbound flight) Flights every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, departing Shanghai at 6:30 AM, arriving in Wenzhou at 8:25 AM, departing Wenzhou at 8:45 AM, arriving in Fuzhou at 10:05 AM, departing Fuzhou at 10:25 AM, arriving in Xiamen at 11:35 AM, departing Xiamen at 11:55 AM, arriving in Shantou at 12:55 PM, departing Shantou at 1:15 PM, arriving in Hong Kong at 2:45 PM, departing Hong Kong at 3:05 PM, arriving in Guangzhou at 3:45 PM. B. (Northbound flight) Flights every Wednesday, Friday, and Sunday, departing Guangzhou at 6:30 AM, arriving in Hong Kong at 7:10 AM, departing Hong Kong at 7:30 AM, arriving in Shantou at 9:00 AM, departing Shantou at 9:20 AM, arriving in Xiamen at 10:20 AM, departing Xiamen at 10:40 AM, arriving in Fuzhou at 11:50 AM, departing Fuzhou at 12:10 PM, arriving in Wenzhou at 1:30 PM, departing Wenzhou at 1:50 PM, arriving in Shanghai at 3:45 PM. The ticket prices have also been set: Shanghai to Hong Kong one-way 200 yuan, round-trip 360 yuan. The ticket prices for the other stations remain the same.

Sino-British Flight, Transporting Passengers and Mail

China National Aviation Corporation and British Imperial Airways have agreed that, starting from the 5th, when CNAC's Shanghai-Guangdong flight extends to Hong Kong, British Imperial Airways' Far East route will also reach Hong Kong at the same time, implementing Sino-British official flights. Afterwards, Chinese and British passengers and mail can reach London from Shanghai via the Sino-British connecting route in just 12 days, which opens a new era in the Far East aviation industry. The postage rates are: Shanghai-Hong Kong airmail postage is 2.5 jiao, plus the ordinary postage of 5 fen, for a total of 3 jiao. The airmail postage from China to the UK and other parts of Europe is 1.05 yuan in national currency.

寶華等六絲織廠　工人昨又罷工 128

The Public Society reports that workers from six silk weaving factories in Shanghai's West District on Avenue President Pershing, namely Baohua, Tiancheng, Fuxing, Yucun Yongfeng, Yiyou, and others, previously initiated the establishment of the Third District Silk Weaving Industry Union. However, Tiancheng and Baohua factories dismissed eleven union organizers, including Lü Shaocheng and Xu Housheng, leading to worker dissatisfaction. Representatives were elected to demand the reinstatement of the dismissed workers from the managers of the two factories. This led to conflicts with guards and staff at the Yucun factory, resulting in a labor strike. Subsequently, over sixty worker representatives presented six demands and petitioned party and government authorities. The Municipal Party Committee, after receiving the petition, feared the expansion of the labor unrest. It promptly collaborated with Zhang Chuqiang, a representative from the Social Affairs Bureau, to earnestly persuade both labor and management in each factory to resume work first, and await mediation according to the law for all disputes. Yesterday morning, around 7 a.m., the workers of these factories demanded the payment of back wages from the factory management, but without result. Therefore, around 10 a.m., they resumed the strike. Upon receiving the report, the party and government authorities believed that the repeated occurrences of labor unrest in these six factories were significantly related to social tranquility. In addition to instructing the workers to await handling, they also decided to formally convene both parties on the 5th of this month (Thursday) for mediation according to the law, in order to prevent the prolongation of the labor unrest.

海員黨部請速頒發　整理海員方案 129

The Special Seamen's Branch of the Kuomintang, in order to manage seamen affairs, previously drafted a plan for reorganizing Chinese seamen, requesting the Central Government to order its implementation. The Central Government ordered the Ministry of Communications to review and implement it, but it has not yet been promulgated. Therefore, the party branch has specifically reapplied to the Ministry of Communications for the original plan: (1) Only those seamen who hold a membership certificate from the Chinese Seamen's Union shall be recognized as seamen. (2) Non-seamen shall not be permitted to serve as seamen workers on vessels powered by machinery. (3) When seamen obtain certificates, the local seamen's branches must employ experts with seafaring skills to conduct face-to-face examinations. Only those who pass the examination can be reported to the headquarters for issuance. (4) The examination of seamen shall be conducted through oral tests and practical operations. (5) When companies and shipping bureaus employ seamen, they must consult with the Seamen's Union. The union shall be responsible to the employer. If dismissals or replacements are necessary, they should also be handled in consultation with the union. If employers and the union have any disputes, they may be jointly decided by party and government authorities.

縣屬各區推舉　土地公斷委員 131

Shanghai County is implementing a land value tax this year. Due to excessive land value assessments, there has been local opposition. After repeated meetings and discussions by local associations, a compromise was decided. In addition to the decision to levy the land value tax, the original Land Arbitration Committee will be supplemented by eleven temporary committee members recommended by each district. They will investigate land values and reassess them to ensure fairness. 昨日黎明前後　霖雨暢霈　田疇得此　裨益不尠 138

Before and after dawn yesterday in this city, there was another abundant rainfall, which lasted for a long time. This will undoubtedly greatly benefit agricultural crops. We now record the details as follows:

Abundant Rainfall

In this city, after a small amount of rain fell on the night of September 15, it became sunny and dry from then on, until it rained again on the 1st of this month. However, the amount of rainfall was minimal, and the weather turned sunny again on the 2nd. The fields were eagerly awaiting rain, but this was not enough. Before and after dawn yesterday, there was a sudden downpour, which lasted for a long time, stopping around 8 a.m.

Darkness After the Rain

After the rain, the sky was as dark as ink, and it seemed like dusk was approaching. It was difficult to distinguish people even a few steps away. Vehicles on the streets all drove slowly with their lights on. Shops had to turn on their electric lights to do business. This darkness lasted for about half an hour before the sky began to clear slightly. However, the clouds were still swirling and seemed to indicate more rain. The weather cleared up in the afternoon, and a pleasant rainfall continued late into the night.

長江水續落　航輪減噸行駛　蕪湖水位僅八英呎九　長沙客貨改駿船轉運 139

Since the beginning of autumn, there has been a lack of rain, and the water level of the Yangtze River has continued to fall, making navigation difficult. According to a report from the Customs Surveyor's Office yesterday morning, the water levels at Anqing, Wuhu, and other places continued to fall. Vessels traveling to and from the area can barely navigate the center of the waterway and must reduce their tonnage. The details are as follows, recorded by a reporter from the Ta Kung Pao:

River Water Falls Again

According to a report from the Jianghai Customs Surveyor's Office yesterday morning, the water level of the Yangtze River upstream continued to fall in the past two days: (2nd) Anqing 10 feet 09 inches, Wuhu 8 feet 9 inches; (3rd) Anqing 10 feet 05 inches, Jiujiang 12 feet. Compared to the water levels reported at the end of last month, it has fallen another five or six inches.

Navigation Tonnage Reduced

Since the Yangtze River water level dropped, navigation has been difficult. Currently, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiangshun, Jianghua, Jiangda, Jiangxin, Datong, Kuailli, Jianguo, and other vessels traveling on the Yangtze River line have reduced their cargo and passenger loads to slightly less than 1,500 tons per ship. During navigation, they must follow the deepest water level in the central waterway. If the pilot and captain are not careful, they may run aground on shallow sandbanks. All other Chinese and foreign private vessels on the Yangtze River line have also reduced their loaded tonnage.

Changsha Transshipment

Although vessels from Shanghai to Hankou, Guanqiao, Shashi, and other places can still barely pass through the deep waterways, the water level in Changsha is two feet, making navigation impossible. Currently, passengers and goods from Hankou to Changsha are being transshipped by smaller vessels.

After Car Kills Person, Speeding Away Like a Soccer Ball: Two Female Workers on Their Way to the Factory at Dawn, Suddenly Hit by a Car, One Injured and One Dead, Car Number of Culprit Impossible to Ascertain 148

Yesterday morning around 5 AM, just as a torrential rain was falling, Xu Xindi, a Ningbo native woman residing at No. 35, Lane 1423, Chongye Li, Yangshupu Road, aged 14, and her left neighbor, Du Gendi (also a Ningbo native, aged 14), residing at No. 39, were holding one umbrella and walking from east to west along the side of Yangshupu Road, 190 yards west of Qiwupu Road, intending to go to the Ewo (Jardine Matheson) Cotton Mill to work. Unexpectedly, a car sped from behind, and unable to avoid it, hit both Xu and Du. Xu died instantly due to severe injuries, while Du suffered minor injuries. The car, seeing that an accident had occurred, instead accelerated and fled without a trace. A passerby, Wu Jixiang, caught a glimpse and immediately summoned an ambulance, sending the two women to Renji Hospital. Because Xu was already dead, her body was transferred to the Coroner's Office on Lunn Road for examination. After examination and treatment by a doctor, Du had already left the hospital. Upon receiving the report, the Yulin Road Police Station ordered detective Pan Yunlong to investigate. Since no one had seen the car's license plate, it was impossible to apprehend the driver. A diagram of the accident scene was drawn. Around 10 AM, the First Special District Court dispatched Prosecutor Tang, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, to the scene to examine the body. Du Gendi testified that after she and Xu were hit by the car, the car immediately drove away, so she could not see its license plate, and her waist was still slightly painful. Wu Jixiang testified that he was 43 years old, from Shaoxing, residing at No. 52, Hongyun Fang, Huade Road. At 5 AM this morning, he was on his way to Xiangtai Timber Company for work, walking towards the two women. Not long after the two women passed him, he suddenly heard a loud car sound. He immediately turned around and saw that both of them were already on the ground, and the car was still speeding away. He only saw that the car was black, the license plate was white with black characters, but he could not see the numbers. Xu Mao, the deceased's mother, testified that her husband was no longer alive, and she relied on her daughter's work for a living, so she requested justice. Prosecutor Tang, after hearing the testimonies, instructed the police station detectives to continue investigating the fleeing car. After examination, it was determined that the deceased Xu Xindi had died from injuries sustained after being hit by a car. The body was handed over to her mother, Xu Mao, who signed an agreement to claim the body for burial.

International Research Association Offers Prizes for Overseas Students' Essays 154

In order to encourage overseas students from our country to conduct academic research, the International Research Association has specially offered prizes for essay submissions. The best essays will be translated and published in "English China Quarterly". The topic is "A Study of Civic Training in Soviet Russia, Germany, or Italy". Entrants may choose one country and write in Chinese or another foreign language. They may also choose another topic, but must first obtain permission from the Association. It is planned to award one first prize of 200 national currency, one second prize of 150 national currency, and one third prize of 100 national currency. A judging committee of domestic experts specially appointed by the Association will review the submissions and determine the rankings, awarding the prizes. If the judges believe that the submissions are not up to standard, the Association reserves the right to withhold the prizes. The word count of the submissions should be at least 5,000 words. The deadline for submissions is June 30, 1937. The list of winners will be announced in the Shanghai newspapers and will also be notified by special letter. Submissions should be sent to the International Research Association, Room 421, Xingye Building, No. 406, Jiangxi Road, Shanghai.

Victor Elliot, a foreigner without consular jurisdiction, 38 years old, residing at No. 11, Tongji Li, Fusheng Road, Zhabei, and Victon, an Italian national residing at No. 25, Zhaopu Road, 29 years old, were found to be selling firearms and pistols. Disguise Himself as a Customer

Pretending to be a rogue from the French Concession to contact Victor, intending to purchase the firearms. Mauser Pistol

Stating that each pistol with 200 bullets cost 92 yuan, and first buy ten pistols. Michael said that he had to pay in advance, Detective Huang opened the wallet to pay. Quiet Place

Car Accident Causes Injury and Flight: Cao Guisheng's Foot Crushed 166

Cao A'gen's second son, Cao Guisheng, a farmer from Wujiatang, the third district of Shanghai County, residing in Humin South Zhelu, 14 years old, was taking a farming cow to graze in the fields, and was returning home at 5:40 p.m. the day before yesterday. When crossing the road, suddenly a car sped from the south. The cow heard the sound and jumped non-stop, causing Guisheng to trip and fall to the ground due to the cow rope being shaken, and was unable to avoid it, and was crushed on his right foot by the car. After a long while, he woke up. The driver, seeing that he had caused an accident, fled to the north. Later, Cao A'gen learned about it and rushed to take him home. It was not until yesterday afternoon that he was sent to Shanghai Yiyuan Hospital for treatment. It is said that his right foot bone has been broken, and he may become disabled.
