Ding Huikang Edited and Published "Experimental Pulmonary Therapy": A Summary of the Important Inventions in Pulmonary Therapy in Various Countries in the Last Ten Years 170

Dr. Ding Huikang, Director of the Hongqiao Sanatorium in this city, went to Europe years ago to investigate the anti-tuberculosis facilities in various countries, personally visited the sanatoriums in the North Sea Islands, the Black Forest in Southern Germany, Central European Swiss Alps and Hot Springs, and specially visited authoritative figures in the academic community and famous professors. Based on the on-the-spot investigation, he compiled this book, which not only describes the changes in modern tuberculosis theory and the anti-tuberculosis methods in various countries for general reference, but also comprehensively collects the experimental reports on pulmonary therapy from famous university hospitals and sanatoriums in various countries around the world in recent years, and its important inventions. It can be regarded as a summary collection of experimental reports on pulmonary therapy in various countries around the world in the last ten years. Our country has no special book on pulmonary tuberculosis. This book can not only be used for research by general scholars and for treatment reference, but also allow patients with tuberculosis to understand all the latest treatments and obtain detailed instructions, so as to obtain great assistance and effect on medical treatment and recuperation. The book is now published by the Medical Bookstore at No. 204, Meibai Road, this city. It is divided into five parts: statistics, prevention, immunity, pathology, and treatment. It is a hardcover volume and is priced at three yuan. The Living Bookstore, Author Bookstore, Guangxie Bookstore, etc. in this city, and the Hongqiao Branch at No. 2, Daxi Road are all on sale.

Pressing for Owed Money Leads to Suicide by Drowning: Young Chen Xianghua Loses His Life in Vain; Bao Cunxin and Yan Qixun Are Both Arrested 171

Chen Dongsheng from Ningbo, currently 52 years old, runs the Chenshengji Coal Store at 223 Feihong Road in Hongzhen. His son, Chen Xianghua, 19 years old, was recommended this spring to work at the Zhongnan Coal Ball Factory at 1032 North Chengdu Road. Because Chen Xianghua owed Bao Cunxin from Shaoxing Yuyao 20 yuan in legal tender, Bao Cunxin, along with Yan Qixun from Nanxun, Chen Meixing, and one unknown person, went to the Zhongnan Coal Ball Factory at around 10 AM on the 28th of last month. They forced Chen Xianghua into the Fuxingyuan Teahouse at 953 North Chengdu Road and demanded the 20 yuan he owed. Because Chen had no money to pay, he was beaten by these people, his face

injured and bleeding. They threatened to cause him trouble if he did not pay by the afternoon. Chen, young and inexperienced, returned to the factory and told his colleague, Du Huinan, what had happened. Unexpectedly, at 12:30 PM, Chen Xianghua, because the deadline was approaching and he still had no money, became extremely agitated. He secretly left the factory and disappeared. On October 30th, Zhang Guisheng, a tea server from the Ningshao Company's Xin Ningshao Steamer, delivered a pair of letters to the Zhongnan Coal Ball Factory. The factory people then learned that it was Chen Xianghua's suicide note. It detailed that he was frightened and coerced, and after leaving the factory, he pretended to return to Ningbo and boarded the Xin Ningshao Steamer. He sailed to the vicinity of the Huishan Wharf in Wusongkou and committed suicide by jumping into the river. The letter was entrusted to the Zhongnan Coal Ball Factory to be delivered to his father, Chen Dongsheng. The factory people immediately notified Chen Dongsheng, who reported it to the Xinzha Police Station. Detective Ma Zhongrong was ordered to investigate yesterday. Unexpectedly, Bao Cunxin and Yan Qixun happened to come to the Zhongnan Coal Ball Factory, intending to demand the remaining 10 yuan from Chen Xianghua. They were arrested by the detectives and taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The police station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, charged them with

extortion by intimidation

and attempted fraud according to Article 346 of the Criminal Law and stated the above situation. Chen Dongsheng, the father of the deceased Chen Xianghua, testified that he did not know about his son's suicide by drowning until he received the suicide note. Witness Cao Zengrong testified that he had witnessed the two defendants beating Chen Xianghua's face until it bled. Bao Cunxin confessed that he had known Chen Xianghua for two years. On October 12th of last year, Lu Yin wanted to open a small coal ball shop and invited him to invest 20 yuan, which he paid and had a written receipt for. This time, he was just asking for the money owed and did not intend to intimidate him. Yan Qixun also denied beating Chen Xianghua. Judge Huang Risheng, after reviewing the statements, ordered the two defendants to be detained and scheduled to re-summon witnesses on Saturday of this week for further verification.

Workers Causing Trouble: Detained in Various Places 172

The Hongzhang Cotton Mill at 381 Maigen Road has been experiencing labor unrest since September 28th. Although mediation by party and government organs has not yet found a solution, there have been disturbances at the factory from time to time. Recently, two workers from the factory mistakenly identified a female worker from the Yong'an Cotton Mill as a Hongzhang worker and prevented her from going to work. They were arrested by the police and sent to the First Special Court, which sentenced them to 20 days of detention. Then, the day before yesterday, around 6 AM, another disturbance broke out at the factory. A group of male and female workers prevented the night shift workers from leaving the factory and prevented the day shift workers from entering the factory to work, and they stopped the machines. The factory telegraphed the Gordon Road Police Station, which ordered Detective Lu Gendi and others to rush to the scene. They arrested two female workers, both named Wang Abao (both from Jiangbei, 18 years old), and one Chen Xiaoda. After questioning, it was revealed that they were instructed by male workers Sun Xiangsheng, Shen A'gen, and Xu Awu. The police then arrested Sun and the others and discovered that the workers who had already been laid off from Hongzhang had organized a union at 20 Chongde Alley, Hengfeng Road in Zhabei, and were constantly spreading rumors and inciting unrest. The disturbance that day was caused by these people spreading rumors that the factory would reduce workers' wages by 20%. The workers, being ignorant, were fooled by them. Yesterday morning, they were also sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The police station's lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated the facts of the case and charged them with obstructing freedom according to Article 304 of the Criminal Law. Judge Ye Shengchao questioned each defendant and sentenced the two Wang Abaos and Chen Xiaoda to five days of detention each, and Sun Xiangsheng, Shen A'gen, and Xu Awu to 15 days of detention each as a warning. The Wangs and others accepted the verdict willingly.

Publication of the "Chinese Postal Worker Monthly," Volume 2, Issue 8 176

The "Chinese Postal Worker" monthly, published by the Propaganda Department of the National Postal Workers' Union in Shanghai, has been widely distributed since its launch and is a leading publication in the current publishing industry. In addition to focusing on the study of labor issues, the content of the journal covers topics such as postal services, international politics, and social economics, and is especially appreciated by readers. Key articles in this issue include: "Respectfully Informing Postal Workers Nationwide" by Shusheng, "Requesting Revision of the Selection and Examination Methods" by Xizhang, "Strengthening the Overall Organization" by Zuo Qi, "Suggestions for Implementing Loan Measures for Postal Workers" by Meng Ming, and "The Necessity of Abolishing the Batch Letter Bureau" by Zheng Xingren. The essays include "The Organization and Recent Situation of the International Postal Workers' Federation" by Zhu Xuefan, "Wartime Transportation" by Wei Yifu, "Psychological Construction for Harmonizing Labor-Management Relations" by Wu Zhi, "The Connection Between Social Life and Literature" by Ju Zhi, and "The National Labor Conference and the Labor Conditions in Italy and Germany" by Zhu Xuefan. The articles are several thousand words long and are worth reading. Other highlights include the selected small articles, poems, travelogues, and original creations in the literary section, which are particularly outstanding in this issue. "The Chinese Language Scores of Students at the Chinese Postal Worker Correspondence School" continues to be published in this issue. The materials collected in "Postal News" and "Major Domestic and Foreign Worker Events" remain the same, but the compilation has been slightly modified. This is an invaluable reference for those concerned with international postal services and the global labor movement. The magazine is priced low, with all 12 issues for the year costing only one yuan, or one dime for a single issue, postage included. Those interested in subscribing can write directly to the Distribution Department of the magazine at 9, Lane 538, Bazilu Road, Shanghai, and their order will be processed promptly without delay.

Weather Report 182

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong is cloudy and clear all around, with southwest to northwest winds. There is heavy rain in the Yellow Sea and Korea, with gentle cyclones caused by a small low-pressure area passing through and moving northeast-east. The Yellow River Basin is cloudy, with northwest winds and fog in the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the East China Sea are cloudy, with uncertain changes and fog, and southeast to southwest winds, caused by another low-pressure area in Hunan and Jiangxi. Furthermore, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 74.1 and the lowest was 59.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 68.0 and the lowest was 63.1.

The Sauce Garden Industry in Shanghai (A General Overview of Shanghai Industry and Commerce, No. 36) 184

(3) Types of Soy Sauce and Their Production Methods - There are four types of soy sauce: "Double Set," "Set Oil," "Mother Oil," and "Top Oil." The difference lies in the quality of the material. Generally, soy sauce made from one catty of fermented soybeans producing only one catty of soy sauce is called "Double Set." Soy sauce made from one catty of fermented soybeans producing one and a half catties of soy sauce is called "Set Oil." Soy sauce made from one catty of fermented soybeans producing two catties of soy sauce is called "Mother Oil." As for "Top Oil," it is almost entirely made from soy sauce residue. The method of making soy sauce is extremely simple. That is, fermented soybeans are stored in a cloth bag, and the mouth of the bag is tightly tied. Then, the oil is squeezed out with a wooden press, and soy sauce is made. As mentioned before, the quality of soy sauce should be best with "Double Set," followed by "Set Oil" and "Mother Oil," and "Top Oil" is the worst, with a salty and bitter taste. Some sauce gardens, for the sake of profit, often add pure sugar (made from barley malt) to inferior soy sauce to relieve the salty and bitter taste, so as to sell it at a high price. This is what we should pay attention to.

In addition to the above types, there are also "Autumn Oil" from sauce gardens in Zhenjiang and Yangzhou. The best is called "Sanfu Autumn Oil." The sauce gardens in Zhenjiang and Yangzhou focus on making pickles, placing vegetables, radishes, etc., in the sauce. The aged sauce for the pickles, every "dog days" of summer, must be like making new sauce, and then exposed to the sun and dew. The sauce extracted from this re-exposed aged sauce is filtered through a cloth bag and becomes "Fu Oil." If this kind of aged sauce has been exposed to the sun and dew for three "dog days," then the soy sauce obtained is "Sanfu Autumn Oil," and its taste is extraordinarily delicious. The reason is that the raw materials of the sauce are already delicious, and then the deliciousness of various vegetables and melons permeates into the sauce, making it even more delicious. In addition, there are so-called "soy sauce essence" and "some kind of fresh juice" on the market, and there are quite a few differences in quality. One type is manufactured by larger seasoning powder factories when manufacturing flavor powder. They use flour to make gluten, then use hydrochloric acid and other chemicals for decomposition, and after chemical action, the toxic substances are removed to become soy sauce essence, so it is fresh and non-toxic. Another type is made by profiteers who buy the remaining malt residue from flavor powder production at a low price and extract the residual juice from it. Therefore, it often contains several toxic substances and is not hygienic. However, this kind of inferior soy sauce essence is very cheap, so it can be popular on the market. This is what we must distinguish.

Shen Bao National Goods Special Edition

A Contribution

Appraising the Contribution of National Goods 185

— Yang An

Appraising national goods cannot be done merely based on the surface; one must study the content and various relationships before one can obtain accurate results.

First, one should base the appraisal on the principles of the seven classes of national goods promulgated by the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce.

Second, one should study whether the manufacturing technology has reached the point of improvement.

Third, one should compare previous products to see how much progress has been made and how much they have been improved.

Fourth, one should study whether the raw materials used are sourced from domestic production. If not, is it because there are truly no domestic sources?

Fifth, one should study the social value of this product and what benefits it brings to society.

Sixth, one should study whether this product is cheaper and better than similar foreign products and whether it is sufficient to resist foreign products.

Seventh, one should study the supply of this product. There is a place to study whether it is oversupplied or undersupplied.

Eighth, one should study whether this product has reached standardization and can be uniformly produced.

These eight items are the keys to appraising national goods, and everyone must study them carefully.

A Visit to the China Pencil Factory 186

— Liang Tongfang

Every year, the customs reports show that more than ten million dollars flow out of the country. This huge leakage is undoubtedly our fatal wound. Among these more than ten million dollars of leakage, foreign pencils seize our money, also accounting for two to three million yuan. The cost of a mere pencil can accumulate to such an astonishing number. No wonder the invasion of foreign goods amounts to tens of millions or hundreds of millions of yuan.

While foreign pencils are rampantly selling well in our market, the China Pencil Factory, a national goods enterprise, was founded in July of the 23rd year of the Republic. The various national goods pencils produced have the potential to surpass the exquisite and practical foreign pencils.

The China Pencil Factory was founded by Mr. Wu Gengxu with a capital of 50,000 yuan. Mr. Wu is a famous industrialist who studied pencil manufacturing in Japan. He is currently the associate manager and factory director of the factory. The manager is Mr. Zhang Weishi.

On the morning of the 22nd of last month, I paid a special visit to the factory at 276 Xiexu Road, Dapuqiao. Mr. Wu personally received me. According to him, the factory is currently divided into three departments: core wood, core making, and finished product. There are more than 50 workers. Regarding the raw materials for the pencils, the factory tries to use domestic goods as much as possible within the possible range. For example, the clay is sourced from Yixing, the pencil lead is purchased from Zhenjiang, and the wood, except for ordinary pencils which use poplar wood produced in the provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Jiangxi, and Hubei, the excellent wood has to be purchased from the United States due to environmental constraints. All the machines are designed by Mr. Wu and built by the Shunchang Iron Works. The cowhide glue is produced by the Shanghai Chitai Glue Factory, the alcohol is produced by the China Alcohol Factory, and other items such as paint are purchased from the Guohua Industrial Raw Materials Company. Therefore, it can be said that the products produced by this factory are made entirely from domestic raw materials. The factory's products are branded with Ding Pi, Aircraft, National Salvation Aviation, and Primary School Student trademarks. In addition to manufacturing ordinary black pencils, the factory also manufactures various high-grade pencils, drawing pencils, red and blue pencils, copying pencils, crayons, etc., with a daily output of 250 baskets (each basket contains 12 dozen, and the wholesale price is from 1.2 yuan to 7.5 yuan per basket). The sales area covers the whole country, and even the Nanyang Islands and Siam have the footprints of the factory's products. The annual total turnover is about 200,000 yuan. On the one hand, it is indeed because the factory strives for excellence in its products. On the other hand, it is due to the enthusiastic care of all sectors of society and the adoption of national goods, which can block a lot of leakage.

Then, under the leadership of Mr. Wu, I visited the factory workshop. The process of making pencils is that the clay is first washed to remove impurities, and then mixed with pencil lead powder. After drying, it is rolled into thin sheets. After it is hardened, it is made into lead rods, and then a lead core machine is used to make it as thick as the lead core. Then, the lead core is placed in a pottery pot and dried once in a furnace. The two ends of the lead core are cut to the specified length. This is the work of making the lead core. The board part is to first use a grooving machine to dig small pieces of wood into slotted strips for placing the lead core. The pencil lead is placed in the slot, and then other wooden boards are firmly glued on with glue. A machine is used to cut it into a circular or hexagonal shape, and the uneven lengths at both ends are cut off and polished. Then, it is placed in a paint application machine, painted several times, and then printed and packaged before it is completed.

The factory's machinery and equipment are very complete, and it also pays great attention to the welfare of the workers. For example, the factory is equipped with powerful bellows to absorb dust and wood chips in the workshop; workers engaged in powder work are equipped with goggles and mouth covers; machine gears and high-speed saw blades are covered with protective nets or coin covers to prevent danger. Special attention is also paid to worker education. Apprentice refresher schools and labor literacy schools are set up to educate apprentices and female workers. Books and magazines are also provided in the dormitory. Other safety equipment, hygiene equipment, sports equipment, and medical equipment are all perfect. Although the factory was established for a very short period of time, it was able to improve its products with meager resources, compete with foreign goods, and gain considerable power. That kind of hard work and attention to worker welfare is worthy of admiration.

Metals　Green Lead Factories See Activity Again　Raw Silk Sells Well, Price Rises by Two or Three Jiao 203

Previously, due to the situation, the outlet for green lead was limited to the military, and trading by merchants and factories had largely come to a standstill. Recently, the situation has eased, so factories in this city, for practical reasons, have become active in green lead transactions again. It is estimated that a total of six to seven hundred bars have been traded, mainly purchased by yellow ochre factories and paint companies. There were only a few purchases by merchants for inland rivers and the Qingjiang route. The market price is reportedly twenty-six yuan per load (on credit), while spot transactions can be two or three jiao cheaper.

Recently, due to scarce arrivals and brisk sales, the raw silk market has been very good. The market price is six yuan and thirty-four jiao per picul, with another two or three jiao added. However, construction gangs and those from the Four Hankous are giving offers, and the imbalance between supply and demand is causing the trend to become more outstanding. Yesterday, some were sold for six yuan and five jiao. It is reported that the amount of spot goods on the market is particularly scarce, so the outlook for the future is very optimistic.

Sugar Market: Over 20,000 Bags of Dutch Sugar Arrived Yesterday 204

Yesterday, the sugar market trended flat. The guild's opening price for spot No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was 21 yuan and 60 cents. Re-export goods were slightly lower at 5 cents, closing at 6 yuan and 10 cents. Spot No. 4 (J) grade East White sugar was priced at 21 yuan and 68 cents, No. 9 (SH) grade at 21 yuan and 30 cents, and re-export No. 8 (N) grade at 6 yuan and 20 cents. All of these saw transactions. Other prices remained unchanged. Our factory's Zhenji No. 1 fine white sugar was priced at 10 yuan and 50 cents, with No. 1345 following suit. No. 1 grade sugar saw Chaozhou merchants offering Chaoqing at over 70 yuan, with a price of 13 yuan and 20 cents. Several dozen bags of ordinary red cotton sugar were priced at 14 yuan and 50 cents. Yesterday, Chisha Denny imported 19,072 bags of No. 24 coarse white Dutch sugar and 5,020 bags of red Dutch sugar.

North and South Goods: New Black Dates Arriving in Increasing Quantities; Candied Orange Peel Rises by Another Yuan 205

Since the arrival of new black dates, both arrivals and sales have been increasing daily. In total, 4,000 to 5,000 packages have been offered by merchants from various locations. Currently, top-quality Guangfu dates are priced at 35-38 yuan, top-quality Dongchang dates at 32-33 yuan, top-quality Boping dates at 33-34 yuan, top-quality Gaogzhuang dates at 25-26 yuan, second-quality Gaogzhuang dates at 22 yuan, top-quality Gaotong dates at 17-18 yuan, ordinary dates at 14-15 yuan, and second-grade dates at 11-12 yuan. Quality varies.

Candied orange peel from Shantou has continued to arrive in the past few days, with a dozen or so pieces arriving, increasing in cost. Due to the small quantity, the market has tightened slightly. Yesterday's offers were all sold, with prices rising by another yuan compared to the previous session. The quality of the goods is also higher than the previous batch, and the trend is firm and stable.

Silk and Tea: Factory Output Unlikely to Be Excessively Abundant; Silk Prices Seem Difficult to Lower 206

Yesterday, the domestic and international silk markets remained sluggish. Prices for Chinese and Japanese silk products in New York declined uniformly. Japanese silk fell by 1 cent to 83 cents and by 2 cents to 79 cents. Shanghai silk fell by 3 cents, and Guangdong silk fell by 2 cents. At the exchange, near-term sales fell by half a cent, while long-term sales rose by 1 cent. There were no changes in Lyon. Yokohama was closed due to the Meiji Festival. The Shanghai silk market saw very few exports, and user activity was also minimal. Market prices continued to decline slightly by 3-5 yuan. However, observing the general silk factories, many are gradually suspending operations due to a lack of dry cocoons. The supply of factory silk is unlikely to be abundant, so current silk prices may be able to maintain a reasonable level.

New York Silk Market Conditions Were Good in October 207

According to Reuters, reports on various raw silk categories in New York during October showed that Shanghai silk and European silk in the United States performed better than the previous month, except for Japanese silk. At the same time, imports of Japanese silk decreased in October, and inventories of other silk products also decreased, leading to a rise in world silk prices in the second half of October. During the month, Chinese silk exports to the United States increased by 277 bales compared to the previous month. Sales of Chinese silk increased by 821 bales, and Chinese silk inventories decreased by 411 bales. Detailed tables are as follows:

Beard 220

— Junmei

Beards, on the human body, also seem to be something related to appearance. For example, our Chairman Lin's silver beard fluttering, and Dean Yu's face full of thoughtfulness, all fully express their kind, gentle, dignified, and solemn expressions. No wonder some people think that a beard is a symbol of masculine beauty, and in some situations, it does indeed give people this feeling.

Therefore, beards are sometimes regarded as a tool. In the business world, "mature and prudent" is always more likely to gain people's trust than "frivolous and impetuous." Fortune-tellers often grow beards, also for this purpose. As for its style, it is indeed diverse, including "one," "eight," and "public" shapes, and it also changes with the times. It is said that people in friendly countries have a "Beard Club" because beards are also sufficient to express the tendency of their national spirit. The "one-shaped" beard of friendly countries looks somewhat brave, enterprising, and lively, which is by no means accidental. Chinese people grow beards mostly as they please, except for young people who are curious to try.

In old novels, we can often see various descriptions such as "three strands of clear beard" and "five strands of long beard," which are actually just like the white, black, grayish-white, and even red beards acted out in operas, connected into a triangle, to express the loyalty, treachery, bravery, and cowardice of the characters in the play, with the same intention. "Later generations look at today as today looks at the past, and people today are no different from people in the past." Beards are naturally no exception.

There are countless interesting anecdotes about beards in history. Recently, contemporary figures such as Xiong Fenghuang shaved his beard because of his marriage, and Chu Taiji shaved his beard to raise funds for disaster relief through amateur performances. One is about growing old and enjoying the pleasure of an affair, and the other is about being eager for public good and benefiting the poor. Their lingering influence is indeed enough to be remembered as a good story.

A local proverb says: "Nine out of ten pockmarked women are pretty, and nine out of ten bearded men are lecherous." The former refers to women and is only about their appearance from behind, while the latter is unknown why it bears this bad name. It is impossible to trace the original creator. Perhaps, bearded men often fail to win women's favor, so they inevitably vent their feelings through "lecherousness," just a joke.

Wild Chicken 221

— Zhou Xian

"Wild chicken" is a kind of woman in Shanghai, a euphemism for lower-class prostitutes. Checking the definition of wild chicken, it is originally one of the fowl, the so-called "pheasant" that Zilu attacked and smelled three times before eating. Therefore, the name wild chicken is "pheasant prostitute." However, this is used in the writings of scholars. If we speak in a popular way, we always say "wild chicken." Why are these lower-class prostitutes called wild chickens? I am afraid that even if you search through the Twenty-Four Histories, you will not be able to find out the reason.

Although wild chicken is a euphemism for lower-class prostitutes, it is now widely used as an adjective in Shanghai. Anything abnormal or irregular is prefixed with wild chicken. For example, if you open a shop, there are always some regular customers who come to patronize. But in addition to these regular customers, if there are strangers who come to the door, these strangers are called "wild chicken customers." This is even more common in the cosmetic market. Those who rarely call for one or two sessions are called wild chicken customers. Those who occasionally go to the dance hall to buy a one-dollar dance ticket and dance are also a kind of wild chicken customer.

Before cars became popular in Shanghai, the most prominent were horse-drawn carriages. There are two types of horse-drawn carriages: privately owned and rental. At the same time, there is also a type that is nominally privately owned but actually rented out, which is called "wild chicken horse-drawn carriage," just like the current "wild chicken car." Although it pays the black license fee for a privately owned car, it is actually doing the rental business of a white license, its function is only to cater to the vanity of customers. Even more common is the "wild chicken rickshaw." It has the name of a private rickshaw, but the reality of a public rickshaw. When soliciting customers, it speaks in a low voice and takes fares, often sneaking into small alleys, furtively, fearing being found by the police and having its license revoked. However, when pulling customers on the street, the passengers sit high and majestic, who can see through that what they are sitting in is a wild chicken rickshaw?

Speaking of wild chicken, it always seems a bit undignified, and it doesn't seem to leak out from the mouths of adults and gentlemen. However, in recent years, the word wild chicken has gradually invaded the education sector. Look, there are quite a few people here who rent a two-story alley house and call themselves "wild chicken universities" to cultivate young people. In wild chicken universities, you only need to pay the tuition fee according to the regulations, and you don't need to attend classes every day. As long as you pass a considerable amount of time, you can actually wear a square hat. The funniest thing is that the professors who substitute for classes often say to people, unintentionally, "I am playing wild chicken." And the students always call this kind of professor "wild chicken teacher."

Wild chicken, in Shanghai, is all the rage, so our Shanghai is no less than a "wild chicken world."

Just taking a few circles, looking at the thousands of electric lights, as if to resist the authority of this dark night, the lights are more decorated with beautiful girls, no, it should be said pitiful women!

They drag on when they meet someone, "Let's have some fun! Sir!" Looking at their faces covered with thick white powder, and their lips added with deep red rouge, is it beautiful? I dare not say, my eyes only have pity! They are making a full of tactful, clear, delicate sounds calling out, but to me it sounds like a tragic cry from hell on earth.

Thinking of the singing and dancing five years ago, Changmen itself should also feel old!

Collection of Tang Dynasty Couplets 224

— Yun

Lu Liankui, a well-known figure in Shanghai, held a wedding for his eldest son, Jiajun, a few days ago. He arranged the hall in the Central Hotel in advance. At the same time, party and state celebrities, as well as leaders from military, political, academic, and business circles, all presented inscriptions, which were dazzling and spectacular. The most unique of them was the Collection of Tang Dynasty Couplets by the Ten Historians. The words and sentences are ancient and elegant, and the structure is natural, which is truly a unique masterpiece. The original sentences are: "New attire dazzles the beauty of Jiangdong," (Du Shenyan) "Ten gifts must be added to Lu Yichong;" (Pi Longmei) "A small hall by the river nests emerald kingfishers," (Du Meizi) "The color of the building in front of the rocks is hidden in the lattice windows;" (Wang Mojie) "The clouds gather to welcome the joy, and the Star Bridge is full," (Liu Wei) "The fan waves gold, and the jade basket is warmed;" (Han Zhengyao) "The boudoir letter is delayed, the green jade table," (Li Wensu) "The special chant is worthy of the jade lotus;" (Lu Luwang) "Wanting to rely on the green window to peep at Han Shou," (Zhao Guangyuan) "Everyone said that Yingmen obtained Confucius Rong;" (Xu Yonghui) "Silver candles flame before, greedy for happy wine," (Li Qiugu) "The precious pen starts the spring breeze on the strings;" (Li Gongchui) "Butterflies hold fragrant stamens, bees hold pollen," (Li Shangyin) "Dew is like real pearls, the moon is like a bow;" (Bai Letian) "Eyebrows seize the color of daylilies," (Wan Chu) "The fragrance of the leak is far away in a hundred flowers;" (Huangfu Zeng) "Agarwood armor is used to meet the wind," (Li Yishan) "Sewing rain and floating smoke as colored cages;" (Han Yu) "Every time I pass the vermilion gate, I love the courtyard threshold," (Wen Tingyun) "Only should the luan and phoenix be in the wutong tree." (Zhang Xiaobiao) The Ten Historians are Shen Heng, Xie Yuanhan, Zhu Baoying, Lan Yunping, Shang Yanliu, Zhang Qihou, Cheng Zongyi, Ye Xianqi, Song Yude, Gao Yutong. The giver is Zai Yu Zhaijun, the Wang family is a prominent family in southern Anhui, with a profound family learning. This time, the imagination is ingenious and creates a new look, which is greatly praised by the guests. On that day, Zhang Xiaolin was surprised to see it and jokingly said that after ten years, it must be sold at a good price. (Que Chou)

Swapped Luan and Phoenix 225

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eight: Vows of Heart with a Cup of Water, Weary Words by the Green Lamp, Gold Hooks and Finger Agreements, Red Beans Report Mutual Love

Menglan suddenly blushed and could not answer. Youmei said: The question I asked is very abrupt. But I am doing it with good intentions. I complain that my learning is not as good as yours, so in literature, I cannot be your confidant. Suppose my learning is the same as yours, or even better, then I would definitely be able to comfort you. How to say it? The ten thousand points of grievances in your heart, someone in the universe knows. But since I can't do it, I think it is not difficult to find such a person in the universe. Tell me the truth, so that I can help you. In writing, is there anyone you admire in your heart? Menglan still held the fan on her face, looking at Youmei. Youmei said: In my life, all my private matters have been told to you, and you have told me mine. You don't think that my temperament has changed and that I am no longer your close friend. Why do you have to suffocate all your suffering in your heart? It would be good to spit out ten points to me. Menglan thought for a long time, suddenly stood up, walked to him, held his hand and said: Mei, save me. With just this sentence, his voice hardened, and two lines of tears flowed, breaking the shallow powder marks on his cheeks and dripping onto his clothes. Youmei immediately stood up, patted his shoulder, and held his hand back, sincerely saying: Just say it, if I can save you, I will definitely save you. Menglan shook her head and said: My heart is messed up, I just feel that I can't say it for a while. Youmei pulled him to sit on the rattan chair, sat slightly leaning on the chair, took out a handkerchief from his body, gently pressed on his eyes, and whispered: Don't be sad. We women who are born in this transitional era are always inevitably sacrificed. But people are not grass and trees, who can be emotionless? If we can avoid being sacrificed, wouldn't it be better? Menglan waited for the tears to dry. Only then did she say: I think, I can't hide this matter from you. And my elder brother also knows about this matter, can you help me? Youmei said: This is the end of it, it can be seen that what I said that I can help you will never be an empty word. Tell me slowly, Menglan said: You probably know a few points, otherwise, you wouldn't come to me and ask me like this. Yesterday I went to find you, you were not at home, I thought that this matter would be known to you. It's not that I didn't tell you, such a good friend, it's really because I regret it very much, I want to escape this heavy net. Saying that, she quietly sighed. (94)

Late Autumn's Yunzao Creek 226

— Ya Fei

The charming autumn sun is coquettishly spreading over the grassland, as if carrying a bit of early spring flavor; the wind, like a pair of amorous young woman's slender hands, surrounded my neck and probed into my chest, making me feel endless comfort and lightness.

A group of three people got off the bus at Yunzao Creek and walked along the river bank. Silently, everyone was temporarily silent, letting the soles of their shoes rub against the fine stones, making a crisp pace, rhythmically rippling in the quiet air, rippling. Rumble rumble! A small train flew past us, and the two rails left behind stretched in front of us like two ink lines, all the way to the horizon, to the end of the sea, and to the end of the world.

After passing the foreign bridge, the river was densely packed with many cargo ships and square-headed boats. On the shore, you could also see some untidy people and scattered small stalls; a group of children were sitting around on the muddy ground talking about something. Everyone was holding a small paper flag in their hands, looking a bit like they were holding a meeting. Rong went to a stall to buy some fruits and snacks, thinking about going to the river to find a cleaner boat, ready to swim the river once, but after walking a lot of the river bank, the few boats that were seen were too unsatisfactory.

"Boat! Boat! Want to swim the river!" Several hoarse voices were ringing in the river, so we turned our heads to look at the place where the sound was ringing, and saw several old women standing on the boat beckoning to us.

"That's not a boat girl, it's simply a boat old woman," Rong said with a humorous tone. Ling was feeling disappointed. She went forward without saying a word. However, I also followed them aimlessly, to see what kind of miracle they would discover today! At this time, I was like a philosopher, using my attitude of questioning life to observe everything in the world, everything in nature. At the same time, I was also like a psychologist, using my keen nerves to carefully analyze the thoughts and psychology of the two of them.

We ate and talked in the cabin, forgetting the pain of reality, forgetting the terror of the world's major crisis breaking out, only enjoying the momentary comfort in front of us, "stealing half a day of leisure," in this half day we traced the past, experienced the present, and looked forward to the future. Although everything in the past was too disappointing, everything in the present was very vague, and everything in the future was even more frightening to think about. However, we can treat these as a nightmare. At this moment, we may as well look for a little spiritual comfort outside the scope of the dream to make up for the defects in our hearts. Because of that, we should protect our pure souls and never let them be damaged in the slightest.

The flowing waves were calmly flowing, and the white clouds in the sky were quietly flying. A slanting sun, several stacks of rosy clouds, the wind blew the willow threads to dance, and the oars struck the water to create subtle ripples; ah! What a quiet and beautiful painting! However, we do not know whether we are the people in the painting, or the painting in front of us? Even we ourselves are a bit at a loss.

Shanghai Newspaper Local Supplement

The Popularity of "Wang Baochuan" 227

— Wu Ci

Women in China are like a special kind of person. If they cannot ascend to heaven, they must fall into hell. Those who ascend to heaven are of course accompanied by their husbands to dance halls and movie theaters; while those who enter hell are mostly doing the work of horses and cows, or living as widows. Heaven is not something that everyone can ascend to, and hell is not something that most people are willing to enter, so those who are caught in the middle have to try their best to maintain their in-between position.

But maintaining it is very difficult, take economics as an example, needless to say, it must be independent, and economic independence, naturally, you have to find a job, if you have a job, then you use the results of your service to exchange for corresponding rewards. Some places even have organizations such as the Women's Social Service Promotion Association for this purpose.

The women's circles in Beiping have such activities.

We live in Shanghai, so of course we have no way of knowing the results of their activities, but from the news published in the newspapers alone, we can also know one or two things, such as preparing to hold a grand amusement fair at the Beijing Hotel, staging old operas and spoken dramas, and deciding to perform the English drama "Wang Baochuan," and asking Ms. Yu Shan to play the lead role.

What arouses our interest in this news is naturally "Wang Baochuan," but it is not because "Wang Baochuan" is an English drama, and when this drama was staged in London, it caused a sensation among the British royal family to visit it. What we feel a little strange is that a group like the Women's Social Service Promotion Association would perform "Wang Baochuan."

Here, we must first explain the reason why "Wang Baochuan" is successful.

Foreigners' welcome of Chinese operas is not worthy of saying artistic appreciation, it is only the impulse of curiosity. The dramas they usually see are mostly realistic, such as the scenery striving for splendor, the actions striving for realism, and for the sake of urgent life, the expression of the theme is often the most urgent part of life. Now they see the symbolic method of using a horse whip as a horse to ride, and they see the joys and sorrows of Wang Baochuan and Xue Pinggui, which lasts for twenty years. So leisurely, so romantic, they naturally can't help but cheer!

But what do we appreciate "Wang Baochuan" for? And what is the purpose of a group like the Women's Social Service Promotion Association staging "Wang Baochuan"?

Is a figure like Wang Baochuan still an idol worshiped in the minds of modern women? Although it is said that marrying a poor scholar with the status of a prime minister's daughter shows that love does not distinguish between classes, and Pinggui's departure to join the army lasted for eighteen years, Wang Sanniang's suffering in a cold kiln for eighteen years, with her heart as still as water, also shows her steadfastness in love. But such love is not worth emulating.

Wang Baochuan is ultimately a product of feudal society. In Wang Baochuan's era, if a married woman could not live as a widow like Wang Baochuan, she would be subjected to the contempt of all people in society. If she was born in modern times, even in places where feudal forces still remain, because of the progress of the times, the environment would not allow such a figure to exist.

Because, this is beyond human nature.

Then, the Women's Social Service Promotion Association's performance of Wang Baochuan, we can only see that they are intentionally or unintentionally worshiping this figure; we can't think of any other significance. In the 1940s China, some people regarded amateur actors playing Nora as a regression. In fact, Nora should still be shown to Chinese women more often in Chinese society. Otherwise, those women who are stuck in the middle may be crushed to death!

A Journey 228

— Ai Tu

——Selection from Haiyan

I love the coast of the South China Sea, where the ocean's waters spread out, covered broadly with silver-like brilliance. This is a fertile expanse formed by fish and shrimp. Three years ago, I traveled and lodged there. The impression remains deeply etched in my mind. Now, we are revisiting the old place. It was a hazy morning, the third day since we arrived in Taicheng from Guangzhou. I blankly boarded a cloud-piercing long-distance bus, my beautiful, appreciative eyes gazing at the snake-like stretching mountains, the lofty, cloud-inserted peaks, the ancient and serene villages hidden under green forests, and the clear stream waters. Although I haven't slept well due to the travel of the past three or four days, Annie still widened her two clever eyes, watching the captivating scenery from the window. She is accustomed to city life, and once she saw these magnificent mountains and rivers, her heart lightly fluttered. This reminded me of when I was in Jiangnan, looking from the train carriage and seeing an endless plain, dense green grass, everywhere showing a soft and elegant demeanor. But near the South China Sea, it displayed towering, magnificent mountain scenery. Perhaps the local customs and conditions of the South China Sea and Jiangnan differ due to the environment of geography and climate.

After a rapid two-and-a-half-hour long-distance bus ride, we arrived in Shenjing. This is the boundary where Kaiping and Yangjiang meet, and also a corner of Haiyan. However, Haiyan is a remote place with vast land, wealthy people, picturesque mountains, and clear waters. Using this place to represent it is insufficient. Many years ago, when bandit gangs occupied Gudou Mountain, Haiyan was disturbed by these gangs. This Shenjing also served as a bandit den for a long time. Thinking back to those years, how frightening it was! Now, peeking at the outlines of those simple country folk, it seems that their local characteristics are very barbaric. This remote乡 with inconvenient transportation also reveals a more primitive style of people.

To Haiyan Street—our destination—there were still more than fifty li of mountain road to cross. My legs could originally run, but unfortunately, I have been suffering from a foot ailment for three or four months. Annie probably can't walk much either, plus there's luggage. So, Lao He called three sedan chairs, each costing two yuan and fifty jiao in silver. After the price was negotiated, the dozen or so sedan chair bearers scrambled for the job, even tearing my rattan trunk. Although running back and forth on a hundred li of mountain road costs a lot of blood and sweat to earn this little money, in the countryside, this amount is not small. So, the sedan chair bearer who couldn't get the job widened his angry eyes, and a breath of disappointment oozed out.

Sitting in a sedan chair was a first for both Annie and me. In the past, in my imagination, before there were cars, sitting in a sedan chair was certainly a privilege for noble gentlemen, so it must be very interesting. But when it came to us trying it, the bitterness felt was hard to bear. Of course, I am not a narrow humanitarian, but I sympathize with the suffering of these laborers. When I saw that the skin on the shoulders of the sedan chair bearer in front of me was calloused and even broken, with sweat dripping down, struggling to wind through the rugged and narrow mountain road, or the winding and difficult paths, my heart clenched up as if something was pressing on it. At the same time, I wasn't used to sitting in a sedan chair. The solid wooden seat and the up-and-down motion soon made my buttocks sore and uncomfortable. I couldn't catch my breath, and my lungs seemed to be dancing, like a prisoner being tortured. I cursed: Why am I doing this? The slave in front is suffering even more than me! Thinking about it, the beautiful mountains and rivers, the enchanting scenery, I no longer had the heart to appreciate it.

When the sedan chair reached Shasha Pass, we got out and walked because this mountain road was the most dangerous and difficult to travel. Seeing the waterfalls and deep streams from the mountain was also heart-stirring. Annie, on the other hand, kept exclaiming how beautiful it was. This was once the big mountain where huge bandits occupied, and the lovely scenery was captivating enough. It also reminded me of visiting Tianzhu Mountain in Hangzhou. This place can also be compared to the magnificence of Nine Streams and Eighteen Gullies. It's a pity that Annie hasn't been to Hangzhou, so she probably doesn't feel that bit of similarity. From now on, Annie will also be living that kind of wandering life. Perhaps, one day, she will have more sweet and bitter experiences.

When the sedan chair reached Wencun, it was almost dusk. There were still nine li of Pingyang road to go. The two sedan chair bearers of Lao He ran particularly slowly. At that time, wind and rain suddenly came. When we arrived at Haiyan Street, it was completely dark. The pale yellow electric lights were flickering. From the time we left in the morning until now, the difficult journey of one hundred and fifty li had emptied our stomachs.

But Haiyan Street—still cherished in my dreams—the kingdom of the sea, my father quietly threw himself into her embrace.

Returning Sails at Sea 229

— Xia Lisi

"The setting sun shines on the red returning sails, drifting on the distant sea; oh, bring my beloved one back safe and sound!..."

Every time such a song rises on the seashore, Louisa, with her beautiful hair flowing, bare feet, and chest held high against the wind, stands on the granite, waiting for someone with ardent expectation—

This person is Gomi.

Gomi is now spreading his unusually strong arms, standing on the bow, with the setting sun, about to sink into the sea, behind him. Under the reflection of the setting sun, he has a bronze complexion and prominent muscles. "Strong Gomi," who on the island doesn't praise him like that? And Louisa, when she is held by Gomi's powerful arms and walks past every household's door on the island, she feels extraordinarily proud! Gomi naturally loves this rough, yet very beautiful, stimulating Louisa: the thought that he is about to meet this wild girl makes his heart blossom with joy.

However, as the ship gets closer to the coast, the women's chorus becomes even crisper in Gomi's ears; as he listens, his face gradually sinks.

"............

Tomorrow we will get married, and he will never go to sea again.

As the wind blows straight into Gomi's heart, a melancholy color flies onto the brow of this strong man—

--Tomorrow we will get married? Yes, Louisa, I have promised you that, saying that this time I come back, I will definitely not go to sea again. But, Louisa, that is still our young people's dream! I didn't get pearls and corals at sea, just brought back a boat of fish. These fish are the shipowner's, what else can I get besides my salary? And what will I use to marry you, Louisa?

On this side, Louisa, who is so excited that she is about to burst, has already left the granite-paved pier and run barefoot to the beach. She is singing along with the melodious song, opening her beautiful eyes wide, and stretching out her right hand to wave at the sails, waving, waving...

--Tomorrow we are really getting married, Gomi! When you went out to sea, didn't you hold my hand tightly and tell me that this time when you come back, we will have a comfortable home? Yes, I am eager to have a home! Gomi, I am really dying of anxiety!

The ship is closer, the sun only leaves a line of golden afterglow, sinking its head into the sea. People are calling each other's relatives' names, the voice of the white-haired old grandmother is even sharper, calling:

"Peter, my good grandson, you are--finally--back safe!"

Then she saw Peter rushing down from Gomi's side and throwing himself into her arms. Gomi also temporarily forgot his depression, and found Louisa standing on the side waiting for him. Like a pair of lovers who haven't seen each other for twenty-five years, they hugged tightly. They were both unable to say a word because of excessive excitement! After a long time, Louisa raised her head from Gomi's hairy chest, and said to him with a smile:

"Gomi, let's get married."

"Um--yes, Louisa--we--oh, I'm really happy!"

In the evening, Gomi drank in the hotel until midnight.

The next day, Gomi signed his name again at the shipowner's place, and Gomi's name was still on the list for the next sailing.

Louisa broke down in tears in his arms.

--This is forced by life, Louisa, it's not that I want to leave you... Let me go one more time, I will be back in a few days. Louisa, I won't cheat you... Ugh, why are you always crying? I don't want you--to cry!"

"Why not cry? Gomi, you're leaving again!"

Yes, on a bright morning at the end of October, Gomi and a fleet of sailing ships sailed out of this island again to develop their destiny. As for Louisa, she is waiting, eagerly waiting for the song to float up again on this lonely coast--

"The setting sun shines on the red returning sails, drifting on the distant sea! Oh, bring my lover back safe and sound!..."

The Old Registrar 230

— Mu Ye

I don't know why, when calling the roll, his eyes, looking out from his old-fashioned nearsighted glasses, were always a little blurred, as if a layer of fog separated them. Those young people, shaking blurry shadows in the classroom, he couldn't distinguish who was male and female, nor could he distinguish anyone's face. The face of each person reflected in his eyes was just a yellow-orange blur, and nothing else existed.

He was deeply troubled by this matter, and he cursed himself—why were his eyes so useless, like a blind man? So, in order to be more "dutiful," he held a large roll book, walked to each desk, and then called out each name one by one, and then laboriously marked an "×" with a pencil. So, he had to walk to every table, door to door. Sometimes there was no one in the seat, but he still walked over. When he found that there was no one there, he was buried in a burst of loud laughter.

In this ×× vocational school, he was the oldest in terms of age. It is said that he had a very good "reputation" decades ago, which was naturally his golden age. However, since the "change of dynasty" that he hated the most, he became outdated, to the point that he is now in the position of registrar with the lowest salary among all the teachers and staff in the school, only twenty yuan per month... Whenever he mentioned the past, apart from sighing, he would scold this "present world" until it was completely riddled with defects.

The reason why he was able to work as a registrar in this vocational school was because of his relationship with Principal Liu. He was a fellow villager and had the same surname as the principal. Twenty yuan a month was already a generous courtesy. So, some people rumored (?) that he was the principal's paternal uncle, but no one went into it too deeply.

He was only in charge of calling the roll. He had to call the roll in a dozen classrooms. If the number of students was less, he was also responsible for finding them. Whether it was in the schoolyard or in the dormitory, he had to search everywhere. What a troublesome thing! He thought of what it was like when he taught in a private school. The students were all well-behaved, unlike these young people who were so impetuous, understanding nothing but love between men and women! But what use were these students to him? So, he thought of the principal again. He knew that the principal collected dozens of yuan in tuition for each additional student. In principle, he was determined to: the more the better, and to reject none who came. So, this made him suffer. He repeatedly suggested to the principal that he give the students three laws (the first being "Be on time to enter the classroom"). The principal only listened with his left ear and let it out of his right. He knew that if it was so strict, it would be detrimental to the income.

"Bring the roll book!" Maybe at some point, the principal would be in the mood and want to care about "school affairs," then the old registrar would tremblingly bring the stack of roll books over.

"Too derelict, too derelict." Why are there so many ×'s? Huh? ...How can this work? Is it okay to always be absent? Tell you, I want you to go and call them one by one, but you always... always don't listen... I think you're full! ...Look at the book full of ×××, I ask you, do you think it looks good or not?" Then, with a "bang!" the principal threw the roll book down with force, and walked away angrily!

Here, he picked up the books one by one "...What do students do when they go to the classroom? The teacher doesn't even come, isn't it just a sloppy calculation? ...Anyway, the money is in hand..." He muttered these words in his stomach, --but didn't say them out loud!

As soon as the bell rang, his work began. Because he was not "full," he ran to every classroom, sweating profusely, holding a large stack of roll books, marking "/" signs. On the playground, in the dormitory, ... even in the toilet, he ran all over, as if begging every student who only liked to play and didn't want to go to the classroom:

"Sir, please go to the classroom, okay? My brother is responsible for calling the roll: otherwise, the principal will vent his anger on my brother. My brother is this year, this year, sixty years old, and there are two people in the family! Ugh, old and useless, if the principal gets angry, ... my brother will have to roll away, ... please sir, help me, isn't it the same to play in the classroom? Talk to female classmates (male classmates), or, bring a novel to flip through, right? ...As long as you, sir, are sitting in the classroom, it doesn't matter if you sleep! ...That way, you, sir, are always "present"; then, my brother can also mark an extra "/" on the roll book. This is a win-win, you, sir, will also look good, and my face will also be able to go down, so... this old man of such an age is really too difficult, you, sir, won't be able to bear it..."

He said what he always said, but he didn't care whether they listened or not.

Later, he finally discovered a good method, which was that whether you came or not, the roll book was a uniform "///"! The principal was naturally happy when he saw it.

In the Plains 231

— Qi Ying

Every first and fifteenth of the month, the owner of this manor in the plains would gather all the skilled horsemen and hold a grand horse race, relying on his ample money and his superb horsemanship to win the hearts and beliefs of the masses. However, the manor owner's painstaking efforts always amounted to nothing; watching the trophy being snatched away by a less outstanding old man, the masses supported him in general, and the daughters dressed in red and green called "Old Man" before and after in a delicate voice. Thus, the manor owner was abandoned in a corner of dim solitude by all the people in the venue. In the aftermath of disappointment and embarrassment, he would always prop his chin with his hand, gnash his teeth, and ponder with a pair of rat-like eyes, as if plotting some sinister revenge against the old man.

However, the old man did not believe that there was any sinister or despicable consciousness in this world. He did not even believe that the famous and profitable manor owner would harm him. Whenever people warned him, he would always be so indifferent, shaking his head and saying, "Don't be defensive, I have never seen the things you said in my life!"

So, people stopped warning him. One day, two days,... the matter of the manor owner plotting against the old man also gradually faded from people's memories. The old man also lived peacefully, and people could see the old man and his horse at all times. Suddenly, one day the old man and his horse disappeared. No one saw the old man and his horse all day long. The news immediately spread throughout the entire village. Everyone ran out of their houses in panic, but the manor owner hid quietly in his house. Everyone believed that the old man and his horse had been murdered. So, people drove their horses in different directions to look for the old man in the plains.

It was very late at night before people found the old man. The moonlight in the plains was bleak and tearful. The old man sat on the ground, his head drooping, his hands holding his knees. His beloved horse lay beside him, already dead, with blood flowing all over the ground. At a glance, it was clear that he had been killed. Everyone was choked up and unable to say a word.

Finally, the old man stood up, slowly walked to the side of the horse, trembling, took the whip from the horse's body, carried it on his shoulder, bent over and walked away without saying a word. The old man probably realized that this world had changed a lot, right? (End)

Silvery Desolation (Zhou Xuan)

Silvery Desolation

The north wind howls. Snowflakes flutter. The north wind howls, shouting out the sad tune of life. Snowflakes flutter, stirring up the annoyance of life. Snowflakes, you just keep fluttering. I entrust you, don't be tired. You flutter all night, filling up the roads for travelers. Teaching the alleys and streets to be deserted of people. Have you firmly remembered? My friends, so many footprints go north, south, east, and west. Leaving traces in the snow. Have you carefully observed, recognized the marks? So many streets and alleys, where should one search? The north wind howls. Snowflakes flutter. The north wind howls, a layer of sorrow envelops. Snowflakes flutter, a burst of desolation twines. Let my heart follow the snowflakes. Falling and shattering coldly. Let my song blend with the north wind. Howling fiercely.

However, it has not been edited well as of today (the 3rd). Perhaps a few shots still need to be reshot temporarily, so it is impossible to catch up on the 7th. Taking its place is Yi Hua's "The Treasure Map."

This large-scale set piece film "has a very serious meaning," and the dog star "Pelli" also participates in the performance.

The Star Company's premiere will be held publicly on Thursday morning.

It is rumored that Mr. Huang Tianshi has joined Hua'an as a publicist.

A Scene from "Night Meeting" 237

Golden City will screen it next issue.

"Motherly Love" 238

The film co-starring Lin Chuchu and Li Keng, mother and son, had "Humanity" in the twenty-second year of the Republic, "Life" in the twenty-third year, and "Family Ethics" in the twenty-fourth year. These three dramas not only caused a sensation in society when they were performed, but also consecutively won the top spot for domestic films in these three years. Now, in the twenty-fifth year, the director of Minxin Company, Jin Qingzi, specially wrote the script for "Motherly Love" and invited Lin Chuchu and Li Keng to co-star, and specially invited Ge Zuozhi and seven other stars to co-star. It is undoubtedly the championship film of the twenty-fifth year.

The entire film is immersed in clean emotions and great motherly love, writing about a mother who has been abandoned by her husband, sacrificing everything from her youth to her death to protect her son's life, raise him to adulthood, and cultivate his future. She would rather suffer from the oppression of life, live a lonely life, do hard work, and spend countless energy. Although she is exhausted, she finally achieves her ultimate goal and gets the final comfort.

Especially the amazing performances of Lin Chuchu, Li Keng, and Ge Zuozhi have surpassed their previous achievements. The efforts of the director, supporting actors, and Fang staff have produced the unprecedented harvest of "Motherly Love," which is especially worth mentioning.
